"<p>1.        disappointed (adj) /ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪntɪd /: thất vọng</p>
<p>The singer has promised to refund any disappointed fans.</p>
<p>- disappoint (v) /ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪnt /: thất vọng</p>
<p>I hate to disappoint you, but I'm just not interested.</p>
<p>- disappointedly (adv) /ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪntɪdli/: thất vọng</p>
<p>‘Is that it?’ she asked disappointedly.</p>
<p>Disappointedly we walked away.</p>
<p>- disappointing (adj) /ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪntɪŋ/: thất vọng</p>
<p>The film was terribly disappointing.</p>
<p>This was very disappointing for all the fans watching the game.</p>
<p>They gave a very disappointing performance.</p>
<p>- disappointingly (adv) /ˌdɪsəˈpɔɪntɪŋli/: thất vọng</p>

"<p>1. entertainment (n) /ˌentərˈteɪnmənt / sự giải trí</p>
<p>There will be live entertainment at the party.</p>
<p>It was typical family entertainment.</p>
<p>It was not something you would watch for light entertainment.</p>
<p>- entertain (v) /ˌentərˈteɪn/: giải trí, tiêu khiển, tiếp đãi, chiêu đãi</p>
<p>The aim of the series is both to entertain and inform.</p>
<p>- entertainer (n) /ˌentərˈteɪnər/: người tiếp đãi, người chiêu đãi, người làm trò tiêu khiển (hát, múa... ở các hộp đêm)</p>
<p>Although her acting skills were limited, she was a great entertainer.</p>
<p>We stopped to watch some street entertainers who were performing in the town square.</p>
<p>- entertaining (adj) /ˌentərˈteɪnɪŋ/: làm vui lòng và vừa ý; thú vị</p>
<p>I found the talk both informative and entertaining.</p>
<p>She was always so funny and entertaining.</p>
<p>- entertainingly (adv) /ˌentərˈteɪnɪŋli/: hấp dẫn, thú vị hấp dẫn, thú vị</p>
<p>2.        international (adj) /ˌɪntərˈnæʃnəl/: quốc tế</p>
<p>He spoke of the failure of the United Nations and the international community to prevent the tragedy.</p>

<p>The island now has an international airport.</p>
<p>- internationalization (n) /ˌɪntərˌnæʃnələˈzeɪʃn/: sự quốc tế hóa</p>

<p>The policies are aimed at promoting the internationalization of investment and production.</p>
<p>- internationalize (v) /ˌɪntərˈnæʃnəlaɪz/: quốc tế hóa</p>
<p>The company will focus on raising productivity, serving customers, and internationalizing its business.</p>
<p>There is an increasing demand on unions and works councils to internationalize their activities.</p>
<p>- internationalism (n) /ˌɪntərˈnæʃnəlɪzəm/: chủ nghĩa quốc tế</p>
<p>The Internet's internationalism puts professionals with language skills at a premium.</p>
<p>- internationalist (n) /ˌɪntərˈnæʃnəlɪst /: người theo chủ nghĩa quốc tế</p>

<p>He is a fair-minded man with an internationalist outlook.</p>
<p>- internationally (adv) /ˌɪntərˈnæʃnəli/: quốc tế</p>
<p>She has lectured widely both nationally and internationally.</p>
<p>3.        profession (n) /prəˈfeʃn/ = occupation (n) /ˌɑːkjuˈpeɪʃn/: nghề; nghề nghiệp</p>

<p>- professional (adj) /prəˈfeʃənl/: chuyên nghiệp # unprofessional (adj) /ˌʌnprəˈfeʃənl/: (nói về tư cách, hạnh kiểm) không phù hợp với tiêu chuẩn/ đạo đức nghề nghiệp; (nói về công việc) không chuyên nghiệp; không phải nhà nghề; nghiệp dư; tài tử</p>

<p>- professionalism (n) /prəˈfeʃənəlɪzəm/: trình độ nghiệp vụ, phẩm chất chuyên môn; tài năng, sự thành thạo</p>
<p>We were impressed by the professionalism of the staff.</p>
<p>Their duties were carried out with commitment and professionalism.</p>
<p>- professionally (adv) prəˈfeʃənəli/: thành thạo, một cách đúng nghề nghiệp; bởi một người chuyên nghiệp </p>

"<p>1.        Training (n) /ˈtreɪnɪŋ/: đào tạo</p>
<p>New staff have /receive a week's training in how to use the system.             </p>

<p>4.        Strong-willed (adj) /ˌstrɔːŋ ˈwɪld /: ý chí mạnh mẽ</p>

<p>5.        Ambitious (adj) /æmˈbɪʃəs/: khát vọng lớn</p>
<p>She has some ambitious plans for her business.</p>
<p>The government has announced an ambitious plan to modernize the railway network.</p>
<p>6.        Local (adj) /ˈləʊkl/: địa phương</p>
<p>Most of the local population depend on fishing for their income.</p>
<p>Our children all go to the local school.</p>
<p>Many local shops will be forced to close if the new supermarket is built.                      </p>
<p>7.        Hard-working (adj) /ˌhɑːrd ˈwɜːrkɪŋ/: chăm chỉ</p>
<p>She was always very hard-working at school. </p>

"<p>1.        Appearance (n) /əˈpɪrəns/: vẻ bên ngoài</p>

<p>2.        Greeting (n) /ˈɡriːtɪŋ/: lời chào hỏi ai</p>

<p>4.        C.V (curriculum vitae) /kəˌrɪkjələm ˈviːtaɪ/ (n): bản sơ yếu lí lịch </p>

<p>5.        Past (adj) /pæst /: thuộc về quá khứ</p>

<p>8.        Tourist guide (n) /ˈtɔːrɪst ɡaɪd /: hướng dẫn viên du lịch   </p>

<p>9.        Telephonist (n) /təˈlefənɪst /: người trực điện thoại</p>

<p>15.        Olympic champion (n) /əˈlɪmpɪk ˈtʃæmpiən/: nhà vô địch Olympic</p>

<p>16.        Sports teacher (n): giáo viên thể dục</p>

<p>17.        Teacher’s diploma /dɪˈpləʊmə/: chứng chỉ giáo viên</p>
<p>The Teacher’s Diploma Primary programme has been thoroughly reviewed and adjusted to the new demands of the Nine Year Continuous Education project of the Ministry. </p>
<p>18.        Love story (n): chuyện tình cảm</p>
<p>He entitled the book “Love Story”.</p>
<p>The play is really a love story. </p>
<p>It is a love story set against a backdrop of rural Irish life.</p>
<p>19.        Keep /ki:p/ in the mind: giữ trong đầu, suy nghĩ    </p>
<p>Do you want this photograph back or can I keep it?</p>
<p>Keep medicines in a locked cupboard           </p>
<p>20.        Romantic (adj) /rəʊˈmæntɪk/: lãng mạn</p>
<p>You used to be so romantic, but now you never tell me that you love me.</p>
<p>I suppose he is quite romantic - he sends me flowers on my birthday and tells me I'm looking beautiful and so on.</p>
<p>21.        Congratulation /kənˌɡrætʃəˈleɪʃn/ (n): chúc mừng</p>
<p>He smiled his congratulations and left without another word.</p>
<p>Congratulations on your new job!</p>
<p>22.        Reader (n) /ˈriːdər/: bạn đọc</p>
<p>She's an avid reader of historical novels.</p>
<p>23.        Make less severe /sɪˈvɪr/: làm cho bớt nghiêm trọng</p>
<p>My backache medicine can make it less severe.</p>
<p>24.        Join (v) /dʒɔɪn/: tham gia</p>
<p>A long suspension bridge joins the two islands.</p>
<p>Join the two pieces together using strong glue.</p>"

<p>5.        Mature (adj, v) /məˈtʃʊr/: chín chắn, trưởng thành # immature /ˌɪməˈtʃʊr/: chưa trưởng thành</p>
<p>- maturely (adv) / məˈtʃʊrli/: trưởng thành, cẩn thận; chín chắn; kỹ càng </p>
<p>- maturity (n) /məˈtʃʊrəti/: tính thuần thục, tính trưởng thành, tính cẩn thận, tính chín chắn, tính kỹ càng; (thương nghiệp) kỳ hạn phải thanh toán # immaturity (n) /ˌɪməˈtʃʊrəti/: sự non nớt, sự chưa chín muồi</p>
<p>- maturation (n) /ˌmætʃuˈreɪʃn/: sự chín (trái cây), sự mưng mủ (mụn, nhọt...); sự làm mưng mủ</p>

<p>- determined (adj) /dɪˈtɜːrmɪnd /: đã được xác định, đã được định rõ, nhất định, nhất quyết, quả quyết; kiên quyết</p>

<p>10.        Joy (n) /dʒɔɪ/: niềm vui </p>

"<p>1.        Training (n) /ˈtreɪnɪŋ/: đào tạo</p>
<p>Employees should be given training in safety procedures.</p>
<p>He is good at selling, although he has had no formal training.</p>
<p>New recruits undergo six weeks' basic training at the base.</p>
<p>- train (v) /treɪn/: đào tạo, huấn luyện</p>
<p>We trained our sales force to be sensitive to the needs of customers.</p>
<p>- trainer (n) /ˈtreɪnər/: huấn luyện viên</p>
<p>Her trainer had decided she shouldn't run in the race.</p>
<p>- trainee (n) /ˌtreɪˈniː/: thực tập sinh          </p>
<p>Many companies recruit graduate trainees to train as managers.</p>
<p>2.        Marry /'mæri/ (v) to sb /ˈmæri/: kết hôn với ai đó  </p>
<p>He was 36 when he married.</p>
<p>I don't want to marry Robert.</p>
<p>- marriage /ˈmærɪdʒ/ (n): hôn nhân</p>
<p>All of her children's marriages ended in divorce.</p>
<p>She has two children by a previous marriage.</p>
<p>3.        Ambitious (adj) /æmˈbɪʃəs/: có nhiều tham vọng (về sự thành đạt hoặc tiền tài) # unambitious /ˌʌnæmˈbɪʃəs/:  không ham muốn, không có tham vọng</p>
<p>They were very ambitious for their children.</p>
<p>She plays a competent, attractive young woman stuck with a slovenly and unambitious young man.</p>
<p>- ambition (n) /æmˈbɪʃn/: mong muốn mạnh mẽ để đạt cái gì; tham vọng</p>
<p>He has already achieved his main ambition in life - to become wealthy.</p>
<p>- ambitiously (adv) /æmˈbɪʃəsli/: khát khao, ham muốn</p>
<p>‘Time's Arrow’ is Amis's most ambitiously structured novel.</p>
<p>4.        Humane (adj) /hjuːˈmeɪn/ nhân đạo, nhân văn # inhumane /ˌɪnhjuːˈmeɪn/: không có lòng thương người; độc ác</p>
<p>These regulations ensure the humane treatment of all refugees.</p>
<p>Campaigners claim that the animals are not being kept in humane conditions.</p>
<p>Conditions for prisoners were described as inhumane.</p>
<p>Many people believe factory farming is inhumane.</p>
<p>- human (adj/ n) /ˈhjuːmən/: loài người # non-human /ˌnɑːn ˈhjuːmən/: không phải con người</p>
<p>Contact with other people is a basic human need.</p>
<p>This food is not fit for human consumption.</p>
<p>Non-human (also spelled nonhuman) is any entity displaying some, but not enough, human characteristics to be considered a human.</p>
<p>- humanely (adv) /hjuːˈmeɪnli/: nhân đạo # inhumanely /ˌɪnhjuːˈmeɪnli/: không có lòng thương người; độc ác</p>
<p>The dog was humanely destroyed.</p>
<p>Prisoners are living in inhumanely overcrowded conditions at the jail.</p>
<p>They treated us inhumanely and just threw food at us.</p>
<p>- humanitarian (adj) /hjuːˌmænɪˈteriən/: nhân đạo</p>
<p>They are calling for the release of the hostages on humanitarian grounds.</p>
<p>- humanitarianism (n) /hjuːˌmænɪˈteriənɪzəm/: chủ nghĩa nhân đạo</p>
<p>The party had a revolutionary image but its purpose was grassroots humanitarianism.</p>
<p>I try to convey that humanitarianism or philanthropy doesn't require you to be wealthy.</p>
<p>- humanity (n) /hjuːˈmænəti/: loài người, lòng nhân đạo, bản chất của loài người, nhân tính</p>
<p>All the streets around the temple were just a mass of humanity.</p>
<p>It is because I care about the future of humanity that I'm conducting this research.</p>
<p>She was told her son had died in the service of humanity.</p>
<p>- humankind (n) /ˌhjuːmənˈkaɪnd /: loài người, nhân loại</p>
<p>These advances should be used for the benefit of all humankind.</p>
<p>This could mean a safer future, not just for humankind, but for the planet as a whole.</p>
<p>This could provide new clues about the origins of humankind.</p>
<p>- humanism (n) /ˈhjuːmənɪzəm/: chủ nghĩa nhân văn, chủ nghĩa nhân đạo</p>
<p>Humanism stresses the importance of human values and dignity. </p>
<p>- humanist (n) /ˈhjuːmənɪst /: nhà nghiên cứu khoa học nhân văn; người theo dõi chủ nghĩa nhân văn</p>
<p>She is a liberal and a humanist.</p>
<p>I respected him as a man of exceptional moral stature and a humanist.</p>
<p>- humanistic (n) /ˌhjuːməˈnɪstɪk/: thuộc về chủ nghĩa nhân văn</p>
<p>Humanistic philosophy affirms that knowledge and power come from people and from the nature in which they live. </p>
<p>5.        Mature (adj, v) /məˈtʃʊr/: chín chắn, trưởng thành # immature /ˌɪməˈtʃʊr/: chưa trưởng thành</p>
<p>Jane is very mature for her age.</p>
<p>Although she was older than her husband, she was emotionally quite immature.</p>
<p>He displays very immature behaviour for a boy of 16, running about the classroom and yelling.</p>
<p>Oh, don't be so immature.</p>
<p>He faced looming middle age with selfish immaturity.</p>
<p>- maturely (adv) / məˈtʃʊrli/: trưởng thành, cẩn thận; chín chắn; kỹ càng </p>
<p>However, it is important that we conduct the debate maturely and as openly as possible.</p>
<p>- maturity (n) /məˈtʃʊrəti/: tính thuần thục, tính trưởng thành, tính cẩn thận, tính chín chắn, tính kỹ càng; (thương nghiệp) kỳ hạn phải thanh toán # immaturity (n) /ˌɪməˈtʃʊrəti/: sự non nớt, sự chưa chín muồi</p>
<p>He has maturity beyond his years.</p>
<p>Her poems show great maturity.</p>
<p>She has shown great maturity in her behaviour this term.</p>
<p>- maturation (n) /ˌmætʃuˈreɪʃn/: sự chín (trái cây), sự mưng mủ (mụn, nhọt...); sự làm mưng mủ</p>
<p>Some experts believe we are now seeing the maturation of the computer industry.</p>
<p>6.        Interrupt (v) /ˌɪntəˈrʌpt /: gián đọan</p>
<p>Sorry to interrupt, but there's someone to see you.</p>
<p>- interruption (n) /ˌɪntəˈrʌpʃn/: sự gián đoạn; sự bị gián đoạn, sự đứt quãng, sự ngắt lời</p>
<p>The game continued after a short interruption because of rain.</p>
<p>- interrupted (adj) /ˌɪntəˈrʌptɪd /: phá vỡ sự liên tục của cái gì một cách tạm thời # uninterrupted /ˌʌnˌɪntəˈrʌptɪd /: không đứt quãng; liên tục</p>
<p>She tried to explain what had happened but he kept interrupting her.</p>
<p>I wish you'd stop interrupting.</p>
<p>We had an uninterrupted view of the stage.</p>
<p>7.        Realize (v) /ˈriːəlaɪz/: thực hiện, nhận ra, thấy rõ</p>
<p>The moment I saw her, I realized something was wrong.</p>
<p>I finally came to realize that he would never change.</p>
<p>- realizable (adj) /ˈriːəlaɪzəbl/: có thể thực hiện</p>
<p>He doubted whether the plan was realizable in practice.</p>
<p>- realization (n) /ˌriːələˈzeɪʃn/: sự thực hiện, sự thực hành, sự thấy rõ, sự hiểu rõ, sự nhận thức rõ</p>
<p>As realization dawned, he went pale.</p>
<p>- real (adj) /riːəl/: thật, thực tế # unreal /ˌʌnˈriːəl/: hư ảo, ảo tưởng, tưởng tượng, hão huyền, có vẻ không thật </p>
<p>All the characters are based on real people.</p>
<p>It wasn't a ghost; it was a real person.</p>
<p>The party began to take on an unreal, almost nightmarish quality.</p>
<p>She felt curiously unreal, as if she were in the midst of a dream.</p>
<p>- reality (n) /riˈæləti/: thực tế, tính xác thực; tính chất đúng (như) nguyên bản # unreality /ˌʌn riˈæləti/: tính chất không thực, tính chất hão huyền</p>
<p>She refuses to face reality.</p>
<p>You're out of touch with reality.</p>
<p>- realistic (adj) /ˌriːəˈlɪstɪk/: hiện thực, có óc thực tế # unrealistic (adj) /ˌʌnriːəˈlɪstɪk/: không chân thật, phi hiện thực</p>
<p>It would not be realistic for the Government to demand a pay freeze in the sector at this point.</p>
<p>It is unrealistic to expect them to be able to solve the problem immediately.</p>
<p>They were accused of being unrealistic in their demands.</p>
<p>8.        Tragic (adj) /ˈtrædʒɪk/ bi thảm, bi kịch</p>
<p>- tragically (adv) /ˈtrædʒɪkli/: theo kiểu bi thảm, thảm thương</p>
<p>- tragedy (n) /ˈtrædʒədi/: thảm kịch                                                       </p>
<p>9.        Determine (v)/dɪˈtɜːrmɪn/: xác định</p>
<p>It is difficult to determine when drama first appeared in India.</p>
<p>- determinate (adj) /dɪˈtɜːrmɪnət /: xác định, nhất định</p>
<p>A determinate sentence of imprisonment was imposed.</p>
<p>- determination (n) /dɪˌtɜːrmɪˈneɪʃn/: tính quả quyết; quyết tâm, quyết nghị của một cuộc thảo luận, (pháp lý) phán quyết của quan toà</p>
<p>He fought the illness with courage and determination.</p>
<p>They had survived by sheer determination.</p>
<p>- determined (adj) /dɪˈtɜːrmɪnd /: đã được xác định, đã được định rõ, nhất định, nhất quyết, quả quyết; kiên quyết</p>
<p>The opposition to her plan made her more determined than ever.</p>
<p>- determiner (n) /dɪˈtɜːrmɪnər/: từ hạn định (chẳng hạn some , your , the ...)</p>
<p>Our English teacher taught us about determiners, which identify which particular noun you're talking about.</p>
<p>- determinism (n)/dɪˈtɜːrmɪnɪzəm/: (triết học) thuyết tiền định; thuyết định mệnh</p>
<p>If determinism is true, then we can be morally responsible for our actions, but none of them are right, wrong, or obligatory.</p>
<p>- determinedly (adv) /dɪˈtɜːrmɪndli/: nhất định, quả quyết; kiên quyết</p>
<p>He continued determinedly despite his injury.</p>
<p>She is determinedly optimistic about the future.</p>
<p>- determinable (adj) /dɪˈtɜːrmɪnəbl/: có thể xác định, có thể định rõ, có thể quyết định</p>
<p>During the third month of pregnancy the sex of the child becomes determinable.</p>
<p>10.        Joy (n) /dʒɔɪ/: niềm vui </p>
<p>Her books have brought joy to millions.</p>
<p>- joyfulness (n) /ˈdʒɔɪflnəs/: sự vui mừng, sự vui sướng, sự tràn ngập niềm vui</p>
<p>The movie's characters are memorable for their robust joyfulness.</p>
<p>Her playing infused the music with a sense of joyfulness.</p>
<p>- joyful (adj) /ˈdʒɔɪfl/: hân hoan, đáng mừng</p>
<p>She gave a joyful laugh.</p>
<p>It was a joyful reunion of all the family.</p>
<p>- joyfully (adv) /ˈdʒɔɪfəli/: hân hoan, vui vẻ, vui mừng</p>
<p>They welcomed him joyfully.</p>
<p>- joyless (adj) /ˈdʒɔɪləs/: không vui, buồn</p>
<p>Jane is trapped in a joyless marriage.</p>
<p>- joyous (adj) /ˈdʒɔɪəs/: vui sướng </p>
<p>She could now enjoy the joyous prospect of being reunited with him again.                                                        </p>

"<p>1.        deaf (n) /def/: điếc</p>
<p>She was born deaf.</p>

<p>The noise of the siren was deafening her.</p>
<p>- deafening (adj) /ˈdefnɪŋ/: điếc tai</p>
<p>The team was greeted by deafening applause from the audience.</p>
<p>The noise of the machine was deafening.</p>
<p>- deafeningly (adv) /ˈdefnɪŋli/: ồn đến mức chói tai</p>
<p>The bird screeched deafeningly.</p>
<p>- deafness (n) /ˈdefnəs/: người bị điếc</p>
<p>Measles can cause deafness and blindness.</p>
<p>2.        disabled (adj) /dɪsˈeɪbld /: tàn tật # non-disabled /ˌnɑːn dɪsˈeɪbld /: không tàn tật</p>
<p>We support disabled students in further and higher education.</p>
<p>Jenny has cerebral palsy and, like most disabled children, she attends a mainstream school.</p>
<p>The project brings together over 200 disabled and non-disabled musicians for a series of live performances.</p>
<p>  - disability (n) /ˌdɪsəˈbɪləti/: sự bất tài, sự bất lực, sự ốm yếu tàn tật</p>
<p>We know some students with disabilities may require additional support to participate in summer camps.</p>
<p>The program provides people with intellectual and developmental disabilities opportunities to work as interns to learn job skills.</p>
<p>  - disable (v) /dɪsˈeɪbl/: làm cho bất lực, làm cho không đủ năng lực, làm tàn tật, làm què quặt; làm mất khả năng hoạt động</p>
<p>He was disabled in a car accident.</p>
<p>  - disablement (n) /dɪsˈeɪblmənt /: sự làm cho bất lực, sự làm cho không đủ năng lực, sự làm tàn tật, sự làm què quặt; sự làm mất khả năng hoạt động</p>
<p>The insurance policy covers sudden death or disablement.</p>
<p>3.        mentally (adv) /ˈmentəli/: về mặt tinh thần</p>
<p>Do you have a mental picture of what it will look like?</p>
<p> The actor doesn't match the mental image I had of the character.</p>
<p>The baby is very mentally alert.</p>
<p>Mentally, I began making a list of things I had to do.</p>
<p>- mental (adj) /ˈmentl/: tinh thần, trí tuệ</p>
<p>- mentality (n) menˈtæləti/: trạng thái tâm lý; tâm tính, trí lực</p>
<p>I can’t understand the mentality of people who are unkind to their pets.</p>
<p>4.        prevent /prɪˈvent / sb from doing sth (exp.): ngăn cản ai làm gì</p>
<p>Maddie would have joined the army if an injury had not prevented her.</p>
<p>The government took steps to prevent a scandal.</p>
<p>- preventable (adj) /prɪˈventəbl/: có thể phòng ngừa được</p>
<p>Both causes are preventable with regular maintenance of the pump and by exercising care when applying the cup.</p>
<p>- prevention (n) /prɪˈvenʃn/: phòng ngừa</p>
<p>The organization is committed to AIDS prevention and education.</p>
<p>- preventative (adj) /prɪˈventɪv/: sự ngăn cản, phòng ngừa</p>
<p>5.        demonstration (n) /ˌdemənˈstreɪʃn/: sự biểu hiện</p>
<p>I'll give a quick demonstration of some first-aid techniques.</p>
<p>Police in riot gear dispersed the demonstration.</p>
<p>- demonstrate (v) /ˈdemənstreɪt /: chứng minh, biểu lộ</p>
<p>Our study demonstrates beyond doubt that the play was written by Shakespeare.</p>
<p>The study demonstrates beyond doubt the effectiveness of the new drug.</p>
<p>- demonstrative (adj) /dɪˈmɑːnstrətɪv/: biểu tình, chỉ thị</p>
<p>Some people are more demonstrative than others.</p>
<p>- demonstrable (adj) /dɪˈmɑːnstrəbl/: biểu thị</p>
<p>There is no demonstrable link between the two events.</p>
<p>6.        add (v) /æd /: cộng</p>
<p>The juice contains no added sugar.</p>
<p>- addition (n) /əˈdɪʃn/: phép cộng</p>
<p>All of these technologies are fairly recent additions.</p>
<p>7.        subtract (v) /səbˈtrækt /: trừ</p>
<p>If you subtract 6 from 9, you get 3.</p>
<p>- subtraction (n) /səbˈtrækʃn/: phép trừ</p>
<p>The children are tested on basic addition and subtraction.</p>

<p>The majority of the population is Protestant.</p>

<p>He's a Protestant.</p>
<p>- protestation (n) /ˌprɑːtəˈsteɪʃn/: sự cam đoan; lời tuyên bố long trọng, lời cam đoan, sự phản đối, sự phản kháng, sự kháng nghị; lời phản đối, lời phản kháng, lời kháng nghị</p>
<p>She repeated her protestation of innocence.</p>
<p>Despite his protestation to the contrary, he was extremely tired.</p>

<p>It's a disgrace that the government spends so much on guns and so little on education.</p>

<p>Are educational standards falling?</p>
<p>- educationalist (n) /ˌedʒuˈkeɪʃənl/: nhà giáo, nhà mô phạm, nhà giáo dục học</p>

<p>The tours are conducted in an educative and enjoyable way.</p>
<p>These children have not been exposed to any educative influences.</p>

<p>He's a Princeton-educated Texan.</p>
<p>They were poorly educated and spoke little English.</p>

<p>- capability (n) /ˌkeɪpəˈbɪləti/: khả năng, năng lực</p>
<p>Age affects the range of a person's capabilities.</p>
<p>- capably (adv) /ˈkeɪpəbli/: thành thạo, khéo léo</p>
<p>He managed the conference very capably.</p>
<p>20.        instruction (n) /ɪnˈstrʌkʃn/: lời chỉ dẫn, chỉ thị</p>
<p>Follow the instructions on the packet carefully.</p>
<p>Always read the instructions before you start.</p>
<p>- instruct (v) /ɪnˈstrʌkt /: dạy, chỉ dẫn, chỉ thị cho</p>
<p>I took the pills as instructed.</p>
<p>You were explicitly instructed to wait here.</p>
<p>- instructional (adj) /ɪnˈstrʌkʃənl/: hướng dẫn</p>
<p>The activities are intended to be both interesting and instructional.</p>
<p>There are a range of instructional videos in the library.</p>
<p>- instructive (adj) /ɪnˈstrʌktɪv/: để dạy, để làm bài học</p>
<p>It was a most instructive experience.</p>
<p>It is instructive to see how other countries are tackling the problem.</p>
<p>- instructively (adv) /ɪnˈstrʌktɪvli/: truyền thụ, hướng dẫn</p>
<p>The outcomes of the two experiments were instructively different.</p>
<p>Her time should be more instructively employed.</p>
<p>- instructor (n) /ɪnˈstrʌktər/: huấn luyện viên, người dạy</p>
<p>He worked for a time as an aerobics instructor.</p>
<p>21.        carefully (adv) /ˈkerfəli/: cẩn thận, chu đáo</p>

<p>- carelessly (adv) /ˈkerləsli/: bất cẩn</p>
<p>- careless (adj) /ˈkerləs/: bất cẩn</p>

<p>- operation (n) /ˌɑːpəˈreɪʃn/: sự hoạt động; cách hoạt động; quá trình hoạt động, phép tính; phép toán</p>

<p>Robots can perform surgical operations on humans.</p>

"<p>1.        confirmation (n) /ˌkɑːnfərˈmeɪʃn/: xác nhận                        </p>

"<p>1.        picturesque (adj) /ˌpɪktʃəˈresk/: đẹp như tranh vẽ   </p>

<p>- picturesquely (adv) /ˌpɪktʃəˈreskli/:  đẹp, gây ấn tượng mạnh, (ngôn ngữ học) cực kỳ sinh động, phong phú; có nhiều hình ảnh (văn)</p>
<p>2.        occasion (n) /əˈkeɪʒn/: dịp </p>
<p>- occasional (adj) /əˈkeɪʒənl/: thỉnh thoảng; không thường xuyên, dành cho môt dịp đặc biệt: thỉnh thoảng; không thường xuyên</p>
<p>- occasionally (adv) /əˈkeɪʒnəli/: thỉnh thoảng, đôi khi                                                </p>

<p>- form (v) /ˈfɔːrmæt /: làm thành, tạo thành, nặn thành, huấn luyện, rèn luyện, đào tạo            </p>
<p>5.        persuade (v) /pərˈsweɪd /: thuyết phục  </p>

<p>- persuasion (n) /pərˈsweɪʒn/: sự làm cho tin, sự thuyết phục, sự tin tưởng, sự tin chắc; điều (người ta) tin tưởng</p>

<p>- association (n) /əˌsəʊsiˈeɪʃn/: sự kết hợp, sự liên hợp, sự liên kết; sự liên đới, sự kết giao, sự giao thiệp</p>

<p>14. impressive /ɪmˈpresɪv/ (adj): ấn tượng ≠ unimpressive /ˌʌnɪmˈpresɪv/ (adj): bình thường, không đặc sắc </p>
<p>- impressed /ɪmˈprest / (adj): cảm thấy ấn tượng ≠ unimpressed /ˌʌnɪmˈprest / (adj): không thấy ấn tượng </p>
<p>- impress /ɪmˈpres/ (v): gây ấn tượng </p>

<p>16.        convenient (adj) /kənˈviːniənt /: tiện lợi ≠ inconvenient (adj) /ˌɪnkənˈviːniənt /: bất tiện</p>
<p>- conveniently (adv) /kənˈviːniəntli/: tiện lợi, thuận tiện ≠ inconveniently (adv) /ˌɪnkənˈviːniəntli/: bất tiện, phiền phức</p>
<p>- convenience (n) /kənˈviːniəns/: sự thuận tiện ≠ inconvenience (n) /ˌɪnkənˈviːniəns/: sự bất tiện</p>
<p>17.     certainly (adv) /ˈsɜːrtnli/: nhất định, chắc chắn # uncertainly /ʌnˈsɜːrtnli/: không chắc chắn</p>
<p>- uncertainty /ʌnˈsɜːrtnti/ (n): sự không chắc chắn # certainty (n) /ˈsɜːrtnti/: chắc chắn</p>
<p>- uncertain /ʌnˈsɜːrtn/ (adj): không chắc chắn ≠ Certain/ˈsɜːrtn/ (adj): chắc chắn</p>
<p>18.        fortunately (adv)/ˈfɔːrtʃənətli/: thật may # unfortunately (adv) /ʌnˈfɔːrtʃənətli/: không may </p>
<p>- unfortunate (adj) /ʌnˈfɔːrtʃənət /: không may # fortunate (adj) /ˈfɔːrtʃənət /: may mắn</p>
<p>- fortune (n) fɔːrtʃən/: vận may, của hồi môn, số mạng                            </p>
<p>19.        accept (v) /əkˈsept /: chấp nhận</p>
<p>- acceptability (n) /əkˌseptəˈbɪləti/: tính chất có thể chấp nhận, thừa nhận</p>
<p>- acceptably (adv) /əkˈseptəbli/: chấp nhận được, thừa nhận được</p>
<p>- acceptance (n) /əkˈseptəns/: sự nhận, sự chấp nhận, sự chấp thuận, sự thừa nhận, sự công nhận</p>
<p>- acceptable (adj) /əkˈseptəbl/:  có thể chấp nhận được, có thể thừa nhận, đáng hoan nghênh, đáng tán thưởng                           </p>
<p>20.        glorious (adj) /ˈɡlɔːriəs/: rực rỡ </p>
<p>- gloriously /ˈɡlɔːriəsli/: vinh quang, vẻ vang</p>
<p>- glorify (v) /ˈɡlɔːrɪfaɪ/: tuyên dương, ca ngợi</p>
<p>- glorified (adj) /ˈɡlɔːrɪfaɪd /: tuyên dương, ca ngợi, tôn lên, tô điểm, tô son điểm phấn                                 </p>
<p>- glorification (n) /ˌɡlɔːrɪfɪˈkeɪʃn/: sự tuyên dương, sự ca ngợi                                 </p>
<p>23.        merrily (adv) /ˈmerəli/: say sưa  </p>
<p>- merry (adj) /ˈmeri/: vui, vui vẻ</p>
<p>- merriment (n) /ˈmerimənt /: sự vui vẻ, sự hớn hở; sự vui chơi                                                </p>
<p>24.        spacious (adj) /ˈspeɪʃəs/:  rộng rãi</p>
<p>- spaciously (adv) /ˈspeɪʃəsli/: rộng rãi; có được nhiều chỗ, kiếm được nhiều chỗ</p>
<p>- spaciousness (n) /ˈspeɪʃəsnəs/: sự rộng rãi; tình trạng có được nhiều chỗ, tình trạng kiếm, được nhiều chỗ</p>
<p>- space (n) /speɪs/: khoảng trống, khoảng cách (giữa hai hay nhiều vật hoặc điểm)</p>
<p>25.        assemble (v) /əˈsembl/: tập hợp lại</p>
<p> - assembler (n) /əˈsemblər/: chương trình dịch hợp ngữ</p>
<p>- assembly (n) /əˈsembli/: sự hội họp của một nhóm người vì một mục đích rõ ràng           </p>"
"<p>1.        picturesque (adj) /ˌpɪktʃəˈresk/: đẹp như tranh vẽ   </p>
<p>It was a pretty town with a picturesque harbour and well-preserved buildings.</p>
<p>The town itself is not especially picturesque.</p>
<p>- picture (n) /ˈpɪktʃər/: bức tranh, bức ảnh</p>
<p>Freddy drew/painted a picture of my dog.</p>
<p>We took a picture of the children on their new bicycles.</p>
<p>-                  (v):  hình dung ra, tưởng tượng ra (cái gì)</p>
<p>Picture the scene - the crowds of people and animals, the noise, the dirt.</p>
<p>- picturesquely (adv) /ˌpɪktʃəˈreskli/:  đẹp, gây ấn tượng mạnh, (ngôn ngữ học) cực kỳ sinh </p>
<p>động, phong phú; có nhiều hình ảnh (văn)</p>
<p>The inn is picturesquely situated on the banks of the river.</p>
<p>2.        occasion (n) /əˈkeɪʒn/: dịp </p>
<p>I've met him on several occasions.</p>
<p>- occasional (adj) /əˈkeɪʒənl/: thỉnh thoảng; không thường xuyên, dành cho môt dịp đặc biệt: thỉnh thoảng; không thường xuyên</p>
<p>The occasional sweet treat won't do you any harm</p>
<p>He spent five years in Paris, with occasional visits to Italy.</p>
<p>- occasionally (adv) /əˈkeɪʒnəli/: thỉnh thoảng, đôi khi         </p>
<p>We occasionally meet for a drink after work.</p>
<p>This type of allergy can very occasionally be fatal.                                       </p>
<p>3.        recently (adv) /ˈriːsntli/: mới đây  </p>
<p>The company recently announced plans to lay off one-fifth of its workforce.</p>
<p>She recently completed a follow-up study of participants.</p>
<p>- recent (adj) /ˈriːsnt /: cách đây hoặc trước đây không lâu; gần đây </p>
<p>The Prime Minister discussed the issue during his most recent visit to Poland.</p>
<p>There have been many changes in recent years.                               </p>
<p>4.        formation (n) /fɔːrˈmeɪʃn/: hình thành, kiến tạo   </p>
<p>This dispute led to the formation of a new breakaway group. </p>
<p>- form (n) /ˈfɔːrmæt /: hình, hình thể, hình dạng, hình dáng, mẫu (đơn...) có chỗ trống (để điền vào)</p>
<p>- form (v) /ˈfɔːrmæt /: làm thành, tạo thành, nặn thành, huấn luyện, rèn luyện, đào tạo    </p>
<p>Swimming is one of the best forms of exercise.</p>
<p>Along with talking and singing, drawing must be the oldest form of communication.        </p>
<p>5.        persuade (v) /pərˈsweɪd /: thuyết phục  </p>
<p>She's always easily persuaded.</p>
<p>I'm sure he'll come with a bit of persuading.</p>
<p>- persuader (n) /pərˈsweɪdər/: người thuyết phục</p>
<p>His deep understanding of the issues made him a powerful persuader.</p>
<p>Lucrative contracts are always a powerful persuader.</p>
<p>- persuasion (n) /pərˈsweɪʒn/: sự làm cho tin, sự thuyết phục, sự tin tưởng, sự tin chắc; điều (người ta) tin tưởng</p>
<p>After a little gentle persuasion, he agreed to come.</p>
<p>She has great powers of persuasion.</p>
<p>- persuasive (adj) /pərˈsweɪsɪv/: có sức thuyết phục, khiến nghe theo</p>
<p>There are several persuasive arguments in favour of the move.</p>
<p>He can be very persuasive.</p>
<p>- persuasively (adv) /pərˈsweɪsɪvli/: có sức thuyết phục, khiến nghe theo  </p>
<p>They argue persuasively in favour of a total ban on handguns.    </p>
<p>- persuasiveness (n) /pərˈsweɪsɪvnəs/: sức thuyết phục, tính thuyết phục; sự khiến (ai) nghe theo </p>
<p>His rage can diminish the persuasiveness of his argument.</p>
<p>You have met this young woman and been impressed by her gentle strength and calm persuasiveness.                                  </p>
<p>6.        relax (v) /rɪˈlæks/: thư giãn</p>
<p>After work she relaxed with a cup of tea and the newspaper.</p>
<p>By and large, cooking relaxes me.</p>
<p>- relaxation (n) /ˌriːlækˈseɪʃn/: sự nới lỏng, sự lơi ra, sự giãn ra (kỷ luật, gân cốt...), sự dịu đi, sự bớt căng thẳng</p>
<p>I go fishing for relaxation.</p>
<p>- relaxed (adj) /rɪˈlækst /: thanh thản, thoải mái, không cảm thấy lo nghĩ, không cảm thấy căng thẳng</p>
<p>She seemed relaxed and in control of the situation.</p>
<p>- relaxing (adj) /rɪˈlæksɪŋ/: thoải mái, thư giãn</p>
<p>I find swimming so relaxing.</p>
<p>7.        take photograph /ˈfəʊtəɡræf/: chụp ảnh</p>
<p>-                      (n): ảnh; bức ảnh</p>
<p>My parents took lots of photographs of us when we were small.</p>
<p>We photographed the house to document the damage done by the storm.</p>
<p>- photography (n) fəˈtɑːɡrəfi/: thuật nhiếp ảnh, thuật chụp ảnh; sự chụp ảnh; nghề nhiếp ảnh</p>
<p>Did you see the film about Antarctica? The photography was superb!</p>
<p>- photographically (adv) /ˌfəʊtəˈɡræfɪkli/: như chụp ảnh (về trí nhớ của ai)</p>
<p>thuộc về nhiếp ảnh, dùng thuật nhiếp ảnh</p>
<p>Much Italian art has already been photographically documented by commercial firms.</p>
<p>The telescope at this observatory is used to survey the sky photographically.</p>
<p>- photographer (n) /fəˈtɑːɡrəfər/: người chụp ảnh; nhà nhiếp ảnh</p>
<p>The couple posed for photographers before going back inside.</p>
<p>Photographer Darren Kidd captured the unique atmosphere of the event.</p>
<p>- photographic (adj) /ˌfəʊtəˈɡræfɪk/: (thuộc) thuật nhiếp ảnh; chụp ảnh</p>
<p>They produced a photographic record of the event.</p>
<p>His paintings are almost photographic in detail.</p>
<p>8.        suitable (adj) /ˈsuːtəbl/ for sb: phù hợp với ai đó</p>
<p>The documentary is particularly suitable for classroom use.</p>
<p>- suitably (adv) /ˈsuːtəbli/: phù hợp, thích hợp</p>
<p>I am not really suitably dressed for a party.</p>
<p>- suitability (n) /ˌsuːtəˈbɪləti/: sự hợp, sự thích hợp</p>
<p>There were doubts about his suitability for the job.</p>
<p>9.        refreshments (n) /rɪˈfreʃmənt / bữa ăn nhẹ và đồ uống.</p>
<p>Light refreshments will be served during the break.</p>
<p>Tickets include the price of refreshments.</p>
<p>- refresh (v) /rɪˈfreʃ/: làm khoẻ người, làm tỉnh táo</p>
<p>The long sleep had refreshed her.</p>
<p>The following morning she awoke refreshed.</p>
<p>- refreshing (adj) /rɪˈfreʃɪŋ/: làm cho dễ chịu và thích thú (do mới lạ)</p>
<p>It made a refreshing change to be taken seriously for once.</p>
<p>It’s refreshing to meet someone who is so dedicated to their work.</p>
<p>- refreshingly (adv) /rɪˈfreʃɪŋli/: thú vị; lý thú</p>
<p>The house was refreshingly cool inside.</p>
<p>10.        occupied (adj) /ˈɑːkjupaɪd /: đã có người (sử dụng)</p>
<p>Only half of the rooms are occupied at the moment.</p>
<p>- occupational (adj) /ˌɑːkjuˈpeɪʃənl/: liên quan tới nghề nghiệp </p>
<p>Back problems are an occupational hazard</p>
<p>- occupationally (adv) /ˌɑːkjuˈpeɪʃənəli/: liên quan tới nghề nghiệp </p>
<p>The foundation is a voluntary group made up of people who geographically, socially and occupationally represent the county.</p>
<p>- occupy (v) /ˈɑːkjupaɪ/: chiếm (không gian, thời gian), sinh sống, làm việc </p>
<p>The bed seemed to occupy most of the room.</p>
<p>As the company grew, it continued to occupy more space.</p>
<p>- occupier (n) /ˈɑːkjupaɪər/: người sinh sống </p>
<p>The letter was addressed to the occupier of the house.</p>
<p>- occupant (n) /ˈɑːkjəpənt /: người sinh sống, người đang sử dụng </p>
<p>All outstanding bills will be paid by the previous occupants.</p>
<p>- occupancy (n) /ˈɑːkjəpənsi/: việc đang sinh sống, đang sử dụng </p>
<p>Prices are based on full occupancy of an apartment.</p>
<p>- occupation (n) /ˌɑːkjuˈpeɪʃn/: nghề nghiệp, sự chiếm đóng, sự cư ngụ </p>
<p>Please state your name, age and occupation below.</p>
<p>11.        pleasure (n) /ˈpleʒər/: niềm vui thích</p>
<p>His visits gave his grandparents such pleasure.</p>
<p>Why do so many boys take pleasure in torturing insects and small animals?</p>
<p>-> pleasurably (adv) /ˈpleʒərəbli/: mang lại niềm vui thích; thích thú</p>
<p>He sipped his coffee pleasurably.</p>
<p>- pleasurable (adj) /ˈpleʒərəbl/: mang lại niềm vui thích; thích thú</p>
<p>We do everything we can to make your trip pleasurable.</p>
<p>12.        sacred (adj) /ˈseɪkrɪd /: thiêng liêng</p>
<p>Cows are sacred to Hindus.</p>
<p>- sacredness (n) /ˈseɪkrɪdnəs/: tính thần thánh; tính thiêng liêng, sự long trọng; tính chất quan trọng</p>
<p>I believe in the sacredness of all life.</p>
<p>The church tries to maintain an atmosphere of sacredness.</p>
<p>13.        associated (adj) /əˈsəʊsieɪtɪd /: kết hợp</p>
<p>The conference will address the broad issues associated with E-commerce.</p>
<p>The following factors were significantly associated with chronic fatigue.</p>
<p>- associate (n) /əˈsəʊsiət: người cùng cộng tác; đồng minh</p>
<p>The company is called Landor Associates.</p>
<p>He was known to be one of the convicted man’s associates.</p>
<p>-                (v): kết giao, kết hợp, liên hợp, liên kết; cho gia nhập, cho cộng tác</p>
<p>He is closely associated in the public mind with horror movies.</p>
<p>-                 (adj): kết giao, kết hợp liên hợp; liên đới</p>
<p>She was only the associate producer of the movie.</p>
<p>- association (n) /əˌsəʊsiˈeɪʃn/: sự kết hợp, sự liên hợp, sự liên kết; sự liên đới, sự kết giao, sự giao thiệp</p>
<p>Do you belong to any professional or trade associations?</p>
<p>- associationism (n) /əˌsəʊsiˈeɪʃənɪzəm/: thuyết liên tưởng</p>
<p>Associationism is a theory that connects learning to thought based on principles of the organism's causal history. Since its early roots, associationists have sought to use the history of an organism's experience as the main sculptor of cognitive architecture.</p>
<p>- associative (adj) /əˈsəʊsieɪtɪv/: người theo thuyết liên tưởng</p>
<p>This definition is not commutative, although it still retains the associative property and is distributive over entrywise addition of matrices.</p>
<p>14.     impressive /ɪmˈpresɪv/ (adj): ấn tượng ≠ unimpressive /ˌʌnɪmˈpresɪv/ (adj): bình thường, không đặc sắc </p>
<p>He has an impressive record of 63 wins from 71 fights.</p>
<p>- impressed /ɪmˈprest / (adj): cảm thấy ấn tượng ≠ unimpressed /ˌʌnɪmˈprest / (adj): không thấy ấn tượng </p>
<p>- impress /ɪmˈpres/ (v): gây ấn tượng </p>
<p>- impression /ɪmˈpreʃn/ (n): sự ấn tượng, điều ấn tượng</p>
<p>- impressively (adv) /ɪmˈpresɪvli/: dễ bị ảnh hưởng</p>
<p>- impressionale (adj) /ɪmˈpreʃənəbl/: dễ xúc cảm, nhạy cảm, dễ bị ảnh hưởng</p>
<p>- impressionist (n) /ɪmˈpreʃənɪst /: (nghệ thuật) người theo trường phái ấn tượng</p>
<p>This is an engaging and impressively researched book.         </p>
<p>15.        confirmation (n) /ˌkɑːnfərˈmeɪʃn/: xác nhận</p>
<p>I'm still waiting for confirmation of the test results.</p>

<p>We have yet to confirm the identities of the victims.    </p>
<p>- confirmed (adj) /kənˈfɜːrmd /: ăn sâu, thâm căn cố đế, thành cố tật, kinh niên    </p>
<p>This chocolate dessert is the ultimate dish for confirmed chocaholics.          </p>
<p>16.        convenient (adj) /kənˈviːniənt /: tiện lợi ≠ inconvenient (adj) /ˌɪnkənˈviːniənt /: bất tiện</p>
<p>Fruit is a convenient source of vitamins and energy.</p>
<p>A bicycle is often more convenient than a car in towns.</p>
<p>That’s most inconvenient for me. I’m working that weekend.</p>
<p>- conveniently (adv) /kənˈviːniəntli/: tiện lợi, thuận tiện ≠ inconveniently (adv) /ˌɪnkənˈviːniəntli/: bất tiện, phiền phức</p>
<p>The report can be conveniently divided into three main sections.</p>
<p>She conveniently forgot to mention that her husband would be at the party, too.</p>
<p>The house is inconveniently situated for local schools.</p>
<p>- convenience (n) /kənˈviːniəns/: sự thuận tiện ≠ inconvenience (n) /ˌɪnkənˈviːniəns/: sự bất tiện</p>
<p>We bought some snacks at the convenience store.</p>
<p>We apologize for the delay and regret any inconvenience it may have caused.</p>
<p>I have already been put to considerable inconvenience.</p>
<p>17.       certainly (adv) /ˈsɜːrtnli/: nhất định, chắc chắn # uncertainly /ʌnˈsɜːrtnli/: không chắc chắn</p>
<p>Certainly, the early years are crucial to a child's development.</p>
<p>I'm certainly never going there again.</p>
<p>They smiled uncertainly at one another.</p>
<p>- uncertainty /ʌnˈsɜːrtnti/ (n): sự không chắc chắn # certainty (n) /ˈsɜːrtnti/: chắc chắn</p>
<p>There is considerable uncertainty about the company's future.</p>
<p>He had an air of uncertainty about him.</p>
<p>- Uncertain /ʌnˈsɜːrtn/ (adj): không chắc chắn ≠ Certain/ˈsɜːrtn/ (adj): chắc chắn</p>
<p>They're both uncertain about what to do.</p>
<p>I'm still uncertain of my feelings for him.</p>
<p>I think it was him, but I can't be certain.</p>
<p>18.        fortunately (adv)/ˈfɔːrtʃənətli/: thật may # unfortunately (adv) /ʌnˈfɔːrtʃənətli/: không may </p>
<p>Fortunately, we got home before it started to rain.</p>
<p>Unfortunately, I won't be able to attend the meeting.</p>
<p>I can't make it, unfortunately.</p>
<p>- unfortunate (adj) /ʌnˈfɔːrtʃənət /: không may # fortunate (adj) /ˈfɔːrtʃənət /: may mắn</p>
<p>He was unfortunate to lose in the final round.</p>
<p>Remember those less fortunate than yourselves.</p>
<p>- fortune (n) fɔːrtʃən/: vận may, của hồi môn, số mạng  </p>
<p>Her father made his fortune selling electronics.</p>
<p>She inherited a share of the family fortune.                          </p>
<p>19.        accept (v) /əkˈsept /: chấp nhận</p>
<p>He asked me to marry him and I accepted.</p>
<p>- acceptability (n) /əkˌseptəˈbɪləti/: tính chất có thể chấp nhận, thừa nhận</p>
<p>The social acceptability of smoking varies between countries.</p>
<p>- acceptably (adv) /əkˈseptəbli/: chấp nhận được, thừa nhận được</p>
<p>Children must learn socially acceptable behaviour.</p>
<p>It is perfectly acceptable for you as an employee to say no.</p>
<p>- acceptance (n) /əkˈseptəns/: sự nhận, sự chấp nhận, sự chấp thuận, sự thừa nhận, sự công nhận</p>
<p>He made a short acceptance speech /speech of acceptance.</p>
<p>Invitations have been sent out and 80 acceptances have already been received.</p>
<p>- acceptable (adj) /əkˈseptəbl/:  có thể chấp nhận được, có thể thừa nhận, đáng hoan nghênh, đáng tán thưởng      </p>
<p>Children must learn socially acceptable behaviour.</p>
<p>It is perfectly acceptable for you as an employee to say no.                     </p>
<p>20.        glorious (adj) /ˈɡlɔːriəs/: rực rỡ </p>
<p>We congratulate you on this glorious victory.</p>
<p>This is a glorious chapter in our country's history.</p>
<p>- gloriously /ˈɡlɔːriəsli/: vinh quang, vẻ vang</p>
<p>The show has been gloriously successful.</p>
<p>The ship has been gloriously restored.</p>
<p>The cast moved well and sang gloriously.</p>
<p>- glorify (v) /ˈɡlɔːrɪfaɪ/: tuyên dương, ca ngợi</p>
<p>He denies that the movie glorifies violence.</p>
<p>- glorified (adj) /ˈɡlɔːrɪfaɪd /: tuyên dương, ca ngợi, tôn lên, tô điểm, tô son điểm phấn      </p>
<p>The restaurant was no more than a glorified fast-food cafe.                           </p>
<p>- glorification (n) /ˌɡlɔːrɪfɪˈkeɪʃn/: sự tuyên dương, sự ca ngợi   </p>
<p>He criticized the entertainment industry for the glorification of violence.</p>
<p>Today's ceremony is not a glorification of war, but a sombre warning about its destructiveness.                              </p>
<p>23.        merrily (adv) /ˈmerəli/: say sưa  </p>
<p>She carried on merrily, not realizing the offence she was causing.</p>
<p>- merry (adj) /ˈmeri/: vui, vui vẻ</p>
<p>I was merry after only a glass of champagne.</p>
<p>We had a few drinks and all got quite merry.</p>
<p>- merriment (n) /ˈmerimənt /: sự vui vẻ, sự hớn hở; sự vui chơi    </p>
<p>Sounds of merriment came from the kitchen.</p>
<p>His unusual name has long been a source of merriment among his friends.                                            </p>
<p>24.        spacious (adj) /ˈspeɪʃəs/:  rộng rãi</p>
<p>The hotel rooms are spacious and comfortable.</p>
<p>- spaciously (adv) /ˈspeɪʃəsli/: rộng rãi; có được nhiều chỗ, kiếm được nhiều chỗ</p>
<p>The accommodation is spaciously laid out.</p>
<p>- spaciousness (n) /ˈspeɪʃəsnəs/: sự rộng rãi; tình trạng có được nhiều chỗ, tình trạng kiếm, được nhiều chỗ</p>
<p>White walls can give a feeling of spaciousness.</p>
<p>- space (n) /speɪs/: khoảng trống, khoảng cách (giữa hai hay nhiều vật hoặc điểm)</p>
<p>She talked about the incredible experience of being in space, looking down on the Earth.</p>
<p>25.        assemble (v) /əˈsembl/: tập hợp lại</p>
<p>All the students were asked to assemble in the main hall.</p>
<p>She then addressed the assembled company.</p>
<p> - assembler (n) /əˈsemblər/: chương trình dịch hợp ngữ</p>
<p>There is an increasing tendency for foreign-owned assemblers to supply the market through imports.</p>
<p>- assembly (n) /əˈsembli/: sự hội họp của một nhóm người vì một mục đích rõ ràng    </p>
<p>Some assembly is required.</p>
<p>South Korea voted for its National Assembly this week.       </p>

"<p>1.        Mass media (n) /ˌmæs ˈmiːdiə/: phương tiện truyền thông đại chúng</p>

"<p>1.        Provide (v) /prəˈvaɪd /: cung cấp</p>
<p>This booklet provides useful information about local services.</p>
<p>All meals are provided at no additional cost.</p>

<p>Despite repeated assurances that the product is safe, many people have stopped buying it.</p>

"<p>1.        Population (n) /ˌpɑːpjuˈleɪʃn/: dân số</p>
<p>- populate (v) /ˈpɑːpjuleɪt /: ở, trú ngụ</p>
<p>- popularly (adv) /ˈpɑːpjələrli/: được quần chúng ưa thích, được nhân dân yêu mến</p>
<p>- popular (adj) /ˈpɑːpjələr/: được nhiều người ưa chuộng, được nhiều người ngưỡng mộ, được nhiều người ưa thích; phổ biến, nổi tiếng</p>
<p>- popularize (v) /ˈpɑːpjələraɪz/: đại chúng hoá truyền bá, phổ cập; phổ biến</p>
<p>- popularity (n) /ˌpɑːpjuˈlærəti/: tính đại chúng; tính phổ biến</p>
<p>- popularization (n) /ˌpɑːpjələrəˈzeɪʃn/: sự đại chúng hoá, sự truyền bá, sự phổ cập; sự phổ biến</p>
<p>2.        Development (n) /dɪˈveləpmənt /: phát triển</p>
<p>- develop (v) /dɪˈveləp/: trình bày, bày tỏ, thuyết minh (luận điểm, vấn đề...), phát triển</p>
<p>- developer (n) /dɪˈveləpər/:  thuốc tráng phim, (tin học) chuyên viên thiết kế</p>
<p>- developing (adj) /dɪˈveləpɪŋ/: đang phát triển, trên đà phát triển</p>
<p>- developed (adj) /dɪˈveləpt /: phát triển, mở mang, mở rộng, khuếch trương, làm cho phát đạt</p>
<p>- developmental (adj) /dɪˌveləpˈmentl/: sự trình bày, sự bày tỏ, sự thuyết minh (vấn đề, luận điểm, ý kiến...), sự phát triển, sự mở mang, sự mở rộng, sự khuếch trương, sự phát đạt</p>
<p>- developmentally (adv) /dɪˌveləpˈmentəli/: sự phát triển, sự mở mang, sự mở rộng, sự khuếch trương, sự phát đạt</p>
<p>3.        Portrait (n) ˈpɔːrtrət /: chân dung </p>
<p>- portraitist (n) /ˈpɔːrtrətɪst /: người vẽ ảnh chân dung. người chụp ảnh chân dung</p>
<p>- portraiture (n) /ˈpɔːrtrətʃər/: cách vẽ chân dung, nghệ thuật vẽ chân dung; tập chân dung</p>
<p>sự miêu tả sinh động</p>
<p>- portray (v) /pɔːrˈtreɪ/: vẽ chân dung, miêu tả sinh động</p>
<p>- portrayal (n) /pɔːrˈtreɪəl/: sự vẽ chân dung; bức chân dung</p>
<p>4.        Documentary (n) /ˌdɑːkjuˈmentri/: phim tư liệu</p>
<p>-                               (adj): đưa ra một báo cáo căn cứ trên sự việc về một đề tài hoặc hoạt động nào đó</p>
<p>- document (n) /ˈdɑːkjumənt /: văn kiện; tài liệu, tư liệu</p>
<p>-                  (v): chứng minh bằng tài liệu; dẫn chứng bằng tài liệu </p>
<p>- documentation (n) /ˌdɑːkjumenˈteɪʃn/: sự chứng minh bằng tài liệu; sự dẫn chứng bằng tư liệu, những tài liệu làm bằng chứng</p>
<p>5.        Adventure (n) /ədˈventʃər/: cuộc phiêu lưu</p>
<p>- adventurer (n) /ədˈvent∫ərə/: người thích phiêu lưu, mạo hiểm</p>
<p>- adventure (n) /ədˈventʃər/: cuộc phiêu lưu</p>
<p>- adventuress (n) /ədˈventʃəres/: người đàn bà thích phiêu lưu mạo hiểm; mụ gian hùng</p>

<p>- developmental (adj) /dɪˌveləpˈmentl/: sự trình bày, sự bày tỏ, sự thuyết minh (vấn đề, luận điểm, ý kiến...), sự phát triển, sự mở mang, sự mở rộng, sự khuếch trương, sự phát đạt</p>

<p>15.        Distinctive (adj) /dɪˈstɪŋktɪv/: đặc biệt, đặc trưng</p>
<p>- distinct /dɪˈstɪŋkt / (adj): riêng biệt ≠ indistinct /ˌɪndɪˈstɪŋkt / (adj) không rõ ràng, mơ hồ </p>
<p>- distinctly /dɪˈstɪŋktli/ (adv) ≠ indistinctly /ˌɪndɪˈstɪŋktli/ (adv) </p>
<p>- distinctively /dɪˈstɪŋktɪvli/ (adv): rõ ràng, minh bạch, rành mạch </p>
<p>- distinctness /dɪˈstɪŋktnəs/ (n): tính riêng biệt, tính rõ rệt </p>
<p>- distinction /dɪˈstɪŋkʃn/ (n): sự khác biệt, việc phân biệt, nét đặc biệt </p>
<p>16.        Advantage (n) /ədˈvæntɪdʒ/: sự thuận lợi</p>

<p>- advantageously (adv) /ˌædvənˈteɪdʒəsli/: thuận lợi, có ích ≠ disadvantageous (adj) /ˌdɪsædvənˈteɪdʒəs/: không thuận lợi</p>
<p>- advantaged (adj) /ədˈvɑːntɪdʒd /: có lợi ≠ disadvantaged (adj) /ˌdɪsədˈvɑːntɪdʒd /: thiệt thòi</p>

"<p>1. work (v)  /wɜːrk/: làm việc </p>
<p>- Iˈve got so much work to do (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- What time do you start /finish work? (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- What sort of work are you experienced in? (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>2. think (v) of sth ( think /θɪŋk/ –thought /θɔːt /–thought): nghĩ đến một điều gì đó</p>
<p>- I donˈt think Emma will get the job.</p>
<p>- &quot;Do you think (that) you could get me some stamps while youˈre in town?&quot;</p>
<p>3. crop (n) /krɑːp/: vụ mùa </p>
<p>- The main crops grown for export are coffee and rice.</p>
<p>- After three crop failures in a row, the farmers face starvation.</p>
<p>- Farmers have reported a bumper crop this year.</p>
<p>4. produce (v) /prəˈduːs/: làm, sản xuất </p>
<p>- France produces a great deal of wine for export. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- Red blood cells are produced in the bone marrow. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- I was wondering whether I could produce a meal out of whatˈs left in the fridge. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- Sheˈs asked me to produce a report on the state of the project. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>5. help (v) /help/: giúp đỡ</p>
<p>- How can I help you? (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- I wonder if you could help me - Iˈd like some information about flights to New Zealand. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- My dad said he would help with the costs of (= give part of the cost of) buying a house. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>6. hard (adv) /hɑːrd /: vất vả, gian khổ </p>
<p>- There was a heavy frost last night and the ground is still hard. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- Heating the clay makes it hard. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>7. rice field (n) /ˈraɪsˈfi:ld /: cánh đồng lúa </p>
<p>- The farmer put up the fence to stop people walking across his rice field. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>8. field (n) /fi:ld /: cánh đồng</p>
<p>- The field was planted with citrus trees. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- The dog leaped over the gate into the field. (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>- The field is overgrown with weeds (Cambridge dictionary)</p>
<p>9. to be in need of (adj): thiếu cái gì</p>
<p>- Are you in need of help?</p>

<p>- The instructions were written in simple English.</p>
<p>- Itˈs simple to find our house.</p>
<p>- I want an explanation, but keep/make it simple. </p>
<p>11. mud (n) /mʌd /: bùn</p>
<p>- The bike got bogged down in the mud.</p>
<p>- The police found tyre tracks in the mud.</p>
<p>- My trousers got covered in mud.</p>
<p>12. brick (n) /brɪk/: gạch </p>
<p>- The house was made of bricks.</p>
<p>- The house was surrounded by a high brick wall.</p>
<p>- He threw a brick at the bird.</p>

<p>- Did you manage to get any bread?</p>
<p>- I only just managed to finish on time.</p>
<p>- A small dog had somehow managed to survive the fire.</p>
<p>14. villager (n) /ˈvɪlɪdʒər/: dân làng </p>
<p>- According to the rainfall pattern and the needs of the growing crops, the villagers can use the water when needed.</p>
<p>15. send (v) somebody to school / college /ˈkɔlidʒ/: gửi ai đi học phổ thông / đại học. (send – sent – sent )</p>
<p>- My dad send my sister to college in Ha Noi.</p>
<p>16. technical high school (n): trường trung học kĩ thuật</p>
<p>- Kay studies at technical school.</p>
<p>17. result in (v) /riˈzʌlt /: đưa đến, dẫn đến. </p>
<p>- The fire resulted in damage to their property.</p>
<p>- Icy conditions resulted in two roads being closed.</p>
<p>18. introduce (v) /ˌɪntrəˈduːs/: giới thiệu </p>

<p>- Thereˈs a shortage of cheap accommodation.</p>"

"<p>1. work (v)</p>
<p>- work + Adverb: work independently ( làm việc độc lập)</p>
<p>- My limbs seemed to be working independently of each other.</p>
<p>- work + Noun: work rate ( tỷ lệ công việc)</p>
<p>- Her boss told her she had to increase her work rate.</p>
<p>- Adjective + work : major work ( công việc chính)</p>
<p>- We are planning to carry out major works on the site.</p>
<p>2. manage (v)</p>
<p>- Adverb + manage : sustainably manage (quản lý bền vững)</p>
<p>-All our tropical timber products come from sustainably managed sources.</p>
<p>- manage + Adverb : manage financially (quản lý tài chính)</p>
<p>- She was finding it difficult to manage financially.</p>
<p>- PHRASES: manage on your own ( tự quản lý, tự xoay sở)</p>
<p>- I canˈt manage all this work on my own.</p>
<p>3. field (n)</p>
<p>- Adjective + field: green field (cánh đồng xanh), cultivated field (ruộng canh tác), ploughed field ( ruộng cày)</p>
<p>- I am looking out on the green fields of Shropshire.</p>
<p>- This discovery has opened up a whole new field of study.</p>
<p>- field + Prepositions: a field of wheat ( cánh đồng lúa mì)</p>
<p>- My family has a field of wheat.</p>
<p>4. export (v)</p>
<p>- Adjective + export: mportant export ( xuất khẩu quan trọng), main export ( xuất khẩu chính) major = pricipal export (xuât khẩu chủ yếu), principal</p>
<p>- Coconut is one of the important exports of the islands.</p>
<p>- VERB + EXPORT: boost export (gia tăng xuất khẩu), encourage export (khuyến khích xuất khẩu), expand export (mở rộng xuất khẩu),  promote export (thúc đẩy xuất khẩu), restrict export (hạn chế xuất khẩu)</p>
<p>- That countries plans to restrict the export of arms to certain countries.</p>
<p>- Coffee is one of Brazilˈs main exports.</p>
<p>- EXPORT + NOUN: export crop (mùa vụ xuất khẩu), export goods (hàng hoá xuất khẩu), export business (doanh nghiệp xuất khẩu), export market (thị trường xuất khẩu)</p>
<p>- We are planning to develop our export market.</p>
<p>- Vietnam has many export businesses.</p>
<p>- PHRASES: a ban on exports (lệnh cấm xuất khẩu)</p>
<p>- Goverment places a ban on exports of toxic waste</p>
<p>5. VERB + IMPROVE: continue to improve ( tiếp tục cải thiện, try to ( cố gắng cải thiện)</p>
<p>-The weather should continue to improve over the weekend.</p>
<p>- She is trying to improve their working conditions</p>
<p>PHRASES: aimed at improving sth ( mục tiêu cải thiện cái gì đó)</p>
<p>- It measures aimed at improving government efficiency</p>
<p>6. knowledge (n)</p>
<p>- VERB + KNOWLEDGE: acquire = gain knowledge (lấy kiến thức), apply knowledge (ứng dụng kiến thức)</p>
<p>- The job gave her the chance to apply the knowledge she had acquired at university.</p>
<p>- KNOWLEDGE + PREPOSITIONS: a wide knowledge of antiques (kiến thức sâu rộng về đồ cổ)</p>
<p>- PHRASES: a gap in your knowledge (lỗ hổng kiến thức)</p>
<p>I did some research to fill in the gaps in my knowledge.</p>
<p>7. harvest (n)</p>
<p>- ADJECTIVE + HARVEST: bumper harvest = rich harvest(vụ mùa bội thu)</p>
<p>- Weˈve had a bumper harvest of apples this year</p>
<p>- VERB + HARVEST: bring in harvest (mang lại thu hoạch), reap harvest ( gặt hái), get in harvest ( thu hoạch)</p>
<p>- They were busy getting the harvest in. </p>
<p>- We are now reaping the harvest of our hard work last year.</p>
<p>- HARVEST + VERB: fail harvest</p>
<p>- The strawberry harvest failed because of the drought.</p>
<p>- HARVEST + NOUN: harvest time,  harvest festival</p>
<p>- HARVEST + PREPOSITIONS: a good harvest of potatoes</p>"

"<p>1. produce (v) /prəˈduːs/: làm , sản xuất</p>
<p>2. production (n) /prəˈdʌk.ʃən/: sự sản xuất, sự chế tạo</p>
<p>3. product (n)  /ˈprɒdʌkt /: sản phẩm</p>
<p>4. producer (n) /prəˈdʒuː.sər/: người sản xuất, người chế tạo</p>
<p>5. productivity /prəˈdʌktɪv/ (n) : năng suất, hiệu suất</p>
<p>6. productive (adj) /prəˈdʌk.tɪv/: năng suất, hữu ích</p>
<p>7. unproductive (adj) /ˌʌn.prəˈdʌk.tɪv/: không hiệu quả, không năng suất</p>
<p>8. productively (adv) /prəˈdʌktɪvli/: có hiệu quả</p>
<p>9. shortage (n)/ˈʃɔːrtɪdʒ/: túng thiếu</p>
<p>10. short-shorter-shortest (adj)/ʃɔːrt /: ngắn-ngắn hơn-ngắn nhất</p>

<p>12. shorty (n) /ˈʃɔːrti/: lùn, thấp bé</p>
<p>13. shortly (adv) /ˈʃɔːrtli/: tóm tắt, trong thời gian ngắn</p>"
"<p>1. produce (v) /prəˈduːs/: làm , sản xuất</p>
<p>- The factory produces an incredible 100 cars per hour.</p>
<p>- How did you manage to produce a meal so quickly?</p>
<p>2. production (n) /prəˈdʌk.ʃən/:sự sản xuất, sự chế tạo</p>
<p>-  The new model will go into production next year.</p>
<p>-  The Riverside Theatre is used to staging major productions.</p>
<p>3. product (n)  /ˈprɒdʌkt /:  sản phẩm</p>
<p>- The London factory assembles the finished product.</p>
<p> - He works in marketing and product development.</p>
<p>4. producer (n) /prəˈdʒuː.sər/: người sản xuất, người chế tạo</p>
<p>- One thing is for certain - the role of the independent producer is secured.</p>
<p>- Many producers are being forced to cut costs and use cheaper materials.</p>
<p>5. productivity /prəˈdʌktɪv/ (n) : năng suất, hiệu suất</p>
<p>- Climate, and particularly site water balance, largely control the structure and productivity of vegetation.</p>
<p>- He said those benefits include higher productivity, lower turnover, less absenteeism and stronger loyalty from the workforce.</p>
<p>6. productive (adj) /prəˈdʌk.tɪv/: năng suất, hữu ích</p>
<p>- The most productive members of staff are rewarded by financial bonuses.</p>
<p>- The local paper factory has been forced to become more productive or face closure.</p>
<p>- It also affects the productive potential of an economy.</p>
<p>7. unproductive (adj) /ˌʌn.prəˈdʌk.tɪv/: không hiệu quả, không năng suất</p>
<p>8. productively (adv) /prəˈdʌktɪvli/: có hiệu quả</p>
<p>- Their working system is based on the belief that people work more productively in a team</p>
<p>9. shortage (n)/ˈʃɔːrtɪdʒ/: túng thiếu</p>
<p>- There is no shortage of funds.</p>
<p>10. short-shorter-shortest (adj)/ʃɔːrt /: ngắn-ngắn hơn-ngắn nhất</p>
<p>- I promise to keep the meeting short and sweet.</p>
<p>- He is shorter than me.</p>
<p>- This blue pen is the shortest. </p>
<p>11. shortness (n) /ˈʃɔːrtnəs/: sự ngắn ngủi</p>
<p>- He keeps his blond hair cropped almost to military shortness.</p>
<p>12. shorty (n) /ˈʃɔːrti/: lùn, thấp bé, ngắn</p>
<p>- I only ever wear a shorty - no full wetsuits for me.</p>
<p>13. shortly (adv) /ˈʃɔːrtli/: tóm tắt, trong thời gian ngắn</p>
<p>- The text is currently being emended and will be published shortly.</p>
<p>- The police evacuated the village shortly before the explosion.</p>"

"<p>1. century /ˈsent∫əri/ (n): thời kỳ 100 năm; thế kỷ.</p>
<p>- ADJECTIVES + CENTURY:  the 18th /19th /20th /21st century ( thế kỷ 18/19/20/21). the early/mid /late 18th century ( đầu/ giữa/ cuối thế kỷ 18), last century ( thế ký trước), the present century (thế kỷ hiện tại)</p>
<p>- The movie is set in the 18th century.</p>
<p>- The boats were built in the last century.</p>
<p>- The present century has seen the start of international terrorism.</p>
<p>- PHRASES: the beginning of the century (sự bắt đầu của kỷ nguyên), the turn of the century ( bước sang thế kỷ), the end /close of the century ( cuối, kết thúc thế kỷ)</p>
<p>- Coco Chanel was born in France at the beginning of the century.</p>
<p>- The town was expanding at the turn of the century.</p>
<p>- He was writing his books towards the end of the 19th century.</p>
<p>VERBS + CENTURY: date from the 18th etc century ( được bắt đầu, được xây dựng từ thế kỷ 18)</p>
<p>-The present church dates from the 13th century.</p>
<p>2. mystery /ˈmɪstəri/(n): điều huyền bí, điều thần bí</p>
<p>- VERBS: be a mystery, solve /unravel a mystery (giải quyết / làm sáng tỏ một bí ẩn)</p>
<p>- Itˈs a mystery how he got my phone number.</p>
<p>remain a mystery</p>
<p>- The children were given the clues and had to try to solve the mystery. </p>
<p>ADJECTIVES + MYSTERY: a complete /total mystery (hoàn toàn là bí ẩn), an unsolved mystery ( một bí ẩn chưa được giải đáp)</p>
<p>- She said that her husbandˈs disappearance was a complete mystery.</p>
<p>- What happened to her is still an unsolved mystery.</p>
<p>a great mystery (=a big and important mystery</p>
<p>3. sample /ˈsɑ:mpl/ (n): mẫu; vật mẫu</p>
<p>- NOUN + SAMPLE: blood sample ( mẫu máu), soil sample (mẫu đất), a DNA sample ( mẫu DNA)</p>
<p>- He compared the samples with a blood sample from Mr Green.</p>
<p>- They analysed soil samples collected from streams.</p>
<p>- Archaeologists are studying DNA samples from ancient Egyptian mummies.</p>
<p>- VERBS + SAMPLE: Take /collect a sample (lấy/ thu thập mẫu), give /provide a sample ( cho/ cung cấp mẫu). analyse /test a sample ( phân tích / kiểm tra mẫu)</p>
<p>- The study took samples from workers at four nuclear plants.</p>
<p>- > He said he had once fainted when giving a sample of blood.</p>
<p>- All the samples were tested for bacteria.</p>
<p>4. range /reindʒ/ (n): loại.</p>
<p>- ADJECTIVES + RANGE: a wide /broad range = a whole range (một phạm vi rộng) , a large /great /huge /vast range (một phạm vi lớn / lớn / rất lớn / rộng lớn), a narrow/limited range (một phạm vi hẹp / hạn chế)</p>
<p>- The Institute organises talks on a wide range of topics.</p>
<p>- He also supports a whole range of other charities.</p>
<p>- During his career he has run a diverse range of businesses.</p>
<p>- They only had a very limited range of products available.</p>"
"<p>1. undersea /ˈʌndərsi:/ (adj): dưới mặt biển</p>
<p>- We are only just beginning to address ourselves to the extraction of undersea resources. (Hansard archive)</p>
<p>- The undersea search for additional resources is therefore an important activity. (Hansard archive)</p>
<p>2. Pacific Ocean /pəˌsɪfɪk ˈəʊʃn/ (n): Thái Bình Dương</p>
<p>- The Pacific Ocean is a body of salt water extending from the Antarctic region in the south to the Arctic in the north and lying between the continents of Asia and Australia on the west and North America and South America on the east.</p>
<p>4. Atlantic Ocean /ətˌlæntɪk ˈəʊʃn/ (n): Đại Tây Dương</p>
<p>- Atlantic Ocean, body of salt water covering approximately one-fifth of Earthˈs surface and separating the continents of Europe and Africa to the east from those of North and South America to the west. The oceanˈs name, derived from Greek mythology, means the “Sea of Atlas.” It is second in size to the Pacific Ocean</p>
<p>5. Indian Ocean /ˌɪndiən ˈəʊʃn/ (n): Ấn Độ Dương</p>
<p>To the south it is bounded by the Southern Ocean or Antarctica, depending on the definition in use. Along its core, the Indian Ocean has some large marginal or regional seas such as the Arabian Sea, the Laccadive Sea, the Somali Sea, Bay of Bengal, and the Andaman Sea.</p>

<p>8. mysterious /mɪˈstɪriəs/ (adj): khó giải thích, bí ẩn</p>

<p>9. mysteriously /mɪˈstɪriəsli/(v): một cách bí ẩn, khó hiểu</p>
<p>My watch had mysteriously disappeared.</p>

<p>10. exist /igˈzist / (v): đã sống; tồn tại</p>

<p>Few of these monkeys still exist in the wild.</p>

<p>11. existence /ɪɡˈzɪstəns/ (n): sự tiếp tục cuộc sống; sự sống sót</p>

<p>12. depth /depθ/ (n) chiều sâu, bề sâu</p>
<p>Many dolphins can dive to depths of 200 metres.</p>

<p>13. deep /diːp/ (adj): sâu</p>

<p>We are deeply grateful for your support.</p>

<p>16. investigate /ɪnˌvestɪˈɡeɪʃn/ (v) : khám phá, điều tra</p>
<p>The FBI has been called in to investigate.</p>
<p>The case will be investigated in detail to determine whether the claims are true.</p>
<p>17. investigation /ɪnˌvestɪˈɡeɪʃn/ (n): sự điều tra</p>

<p>20. accident /ˈæksɪdənt / (n): tai nạn</p>

<p>21. accidental /ˌæksɪˈdentl/ (adj): tình cờ, vô tình</p>

<p>22. accidentally /ˌæksɪˈdentəli/ (adv): tình cờ, ngẫu nhiên</p>

<p>The damage couldn't have been caused accidentally.</p>
<p>23. entrap /ɪnˈtræp/ (v) đánh bẫy, lừa</p>

<p>25. protect /prəˈtekt / (v) bảo vệ, bảo hộ, che chở</p>

<p>27. protector /prəˈtektər/ (n): người bảo vệ</p>

<p>28. protective /prəˈtektɪv/ (adj): bảo vệ</p>
<p>Workers should wear full protective clothing.</p>

<p>29. protectively /prəˈtektɪvli/ (adv): bảo vệ, bảo hộ, ngăn ngừa</p>
<p>He put an arm around her shoulder protectively.</p>
<p>She held her hands protectively over her eyes.</p>
<p> 30. protectionist /prəˈtekʃənɪst /: người ủng hộ chế độ bảo vệ</p>

"<p>31. pollute /pəˈlu:t / (v) làm ô nhiễm, làm nhơ bẩn (nước...)</p>
<p>The pesticides used on many farms are polluting the water supply.</p>
<p>We won't invest in any company that pollutes the environment.</p>
<p>32. pollutant /pəˈluːtənt / (n) chất ô nhiễm</p>
<p>Sulphur dioxide is one of several pollutants that are released into the atmosphere by coal-fired power stations.</p>
<p>These turning points have become important in debates over regional and global pollutants.</p>
<p>33. polluter /pəˈluːtər/: người gây ô nhiễm</p>
<p>The region's third-largest industrial polluter reduced its emissions by about a third.</p>
<p>The environmental regulation requires the polluters to comply with safe environmental standards.</p>
<p>34. pollution /pəˈluːʃn/ (n): sự ô nhiễm</p>
<p>The manifesto includes tough measures to tackle road congestion and environmental pollution.</p>
<p>The company claims it is not responsible for the pollution in the river.</p>
<p>Car exhaust is the main reason for the city's pollution.</p>
<p>The once azure skies of Athens have been ruined by atmospheric pollution.</p>
<p>The survey shows a link between asthma and air pollution.</p>
<p>Stricter controls on air pollution would help to reduce acid rain.</p>
<p>35. limited /ˈlɪmɪtɪd / (adj) hạn chế, có giới hạn # unlimited /ʌnˈlɪmɪtɪd / (adj) vô hạn</p>
<p>My culinary skills are rather limited, I'm afraid !</p>
<p>I'm afraid my grasp of economics is rather limited.</p>
<p>I only have a limited knowledge of Spanish.</p>
<p>Most people only have a limited amount of leisure time.</p>
<p>36. limit (n) /ˈlɪmɪt /: giới hạn</p>
<p>Is there a limit on the amount of money you can claim?</p>
<p>I think we ought to put a strict limit on the amount of time we can spend on the project.</p>
<p>There's a limit to the number of times I can stop what I'm doing just so I can help him!</p>
<p>We set a time limit of 30 minutes for the test.</p>
<p>37. limitation (n) /ˌlɪmɪˈteɪʃn/: sự giới hạn</p>
<p>Living in an apartment is fine, but it does have its limitations - for example, you don't have your own garden.</p>
<p>Despite her limitations as an actress, she was a great entertainer.</p>
<p>38. threaten /ˈθretn/ (v) doạ, đe doạ, hăm doạ </p>
<p>Greenpeace works to promote awareness of the dangers that threaten our planet today.</p>
<p>Britain threatened to break off diplomatic relations.</p>
<p>A masked robber threatened the bank staff with a gun.</p>
<p>They threatened to blow up the plane if their demands were not met.</p>
<p>She's threatening to take me to court for not paying the bill on time.</p>
<p>39. threatened /ˈθretnd / (adj) bị đe doạ</p>
<p>Five threatened species, including chinook salmon and bald eagles, might also be in the way of the nine-mile pipeline project.</p>
<p>This is why the small family farm is so threatened - it can never be as efficient or produce milk as cheaply as a larger farm with hundreds of cows.</p>
<p>Funds intended for product development were spent on delivering ridiculous pay deals to buy off threatened strikes.</p>
<p>He got wind of a threatened attack.</p>
<p>40. threatening /ˈθretnɪŋ/ (adj): đe dọa</p>
<p>The house seemed less threatening in daylight.</p>
<p>41. threateningly /ˈθretnɪŋli/ (adv): đe dọa</p>
<p>The enemy plane came threateningly close.</p>
<p>Three men stood threateningly over them.</p>
<p>42. endanger /ɪnˈdeɪndʒər/ (v): nguy hiểm</p>
<p>He would never do anything to endanger the lives of his children.</p>
<p>We must be careful not to do anything that might endanger the economic recovery.</p>
<p>43. endangered /ɪnˈdeɪndʒərd / (adj) có nguy cơ tuyệt chủng</p>
<p>Social workers who look after abused or endangered children often have stressful days at work.</p>
<p>44. endangerment /ɪnˈdeɪndʒərmənt / (n): sự nguy hiểm</p>
<p>The problems that have contributed to the endangerment of the species are largely caused by humans.</p>
<p>45. dispose /dɪˈspəʊz/ (v): vứt bỏ, sắp xếp, có sẵn</p>
<p>The visitors disposed themselves in a circle round the statue.</p>
<p>46. disposable /dɪˈspəʊzəbl/ (adj): dùng một lần</p>
<p>The council is responsible for waste disposal and street cleaning.</p>
<p>It is completely wrong for corporations to view workers as disposable.</p>
<p>47. disposal /dɪˈspəʊzl/: chất thải, bỏ đi</p>
<p>The council is responsible for waste disposal and street cleaning.</p>
<p>48. disposed /dɪˈspəʊzd / (adj): sẵn sàng #  indisposed /ˌɪndɪˈspəʊzd / (adj): miễn cưỡng</p>
<p>I'm not disposed to argue.</p>
<p>You're most welcome to join us if you feel so disposed.</p>
<p>being naturally disposed towards speculation.</p>
<p>Large sections of the potential audience seemed indisposed to attend.</p>
<p>49. harmful /ˈhɑːrmfl/ (adj): có hại # harmless /ˈhɑːrmləs/ (adj): vô hại</p>
<p>Many household products are potentially harmful.</p>
<p>Fruit juices can be harmful to children's teeth.</p>
<p>It's just a bit of harmless fun.</p>
<p>The bacteria is harmless to humans.</p>
<p>50. harmfully /ˈhɑːrmfəli/ (adv): có hại</p>
<p>The drug may interact harmfully with other medicines.</p>
<p>Her comments were not only unkind, but harmfully misleading</p>
<p>51. harmfulness /ˈhɑːrmflnəs/ (n): sự có hại</p>
<p>Progress has been slow because of heightened fears over the harmfulness of pesticides.</p>
<p>The harmfulness of these policies is very apparent</p>
<p>52. consequence /ˈkɑːnsɪkwens/ (n): hậu quả, kết quả</p>
<p>Have you considered the possible consequences?</p>
<p>Reform often produces unintended consequences.</p>
<p>They must be prepared to accept the consequences of their actions.</p>
<p>A White House spokesman said that civilian casualties were an inevitable consequence of war.</p>
<p>53. consequent /ˈkɑːnsɪkwent / (adj): hệ quả</p>
<p>Our use of harmful chemicals and the consequent damage to the environment is a very serious matter.</p>
<p>54. consequential/ˌkɑːnsɪˈkwenʃl/ (adj): hậu quả đáng kể # inconsequential /ɪnˌkɑːnsɪˈkwenʃl/ (adj): không đáng kể</p>
<p>Most of what she said was pretty inconsequential.</p>
<p>We ssuffererd a consequential loss as a result of the non-delivery of these documents and intend to claim compensation.</p>
<p>55. consequentially /ˈkɑːnsɪkwentli/ (adv): do đó</p>
<p>That is already something which rests upon their shoulders vicariously and consequentially, so why add this to it?</p>
<p>56. explosive /ɪkˈspləʊsɪv/ (adj, n) chất nổ</p>
<p>The political situation is potentially explosive.</p>
<p>Hydrogen is highly explosive.</p>
<p>57. explosively /ɪkˈspləʊsɪvli/: bùng nổ</p>
<p>During our conversation he sometimes giggles explosively.</p>
<p>As a player he was talented and explosively energetic.</p>"

"<p>1.        leopard (n) /ˈlepərd /: con báo</p>

<p>8. destructible /dɪˈstrʌktəbl/ (adj): có thể phá hủy, có thể mất hiệu lực</p>

<p>Salary scales vary between states/from state to state /according to state /with each state.</p>
<p>The samples varied in quality but were generally acceptable.</p>
<p>We have tried several different approaches, with varying degrees of success.</p>

"<p>1. flexible (adj) /ˈfleksəbl/: linh họat, dễ sai khiến</p>
<p>The European Union should remain flexible enough to assimilate more countries quickly.</p>
<p>&quot;If they're flexible, we're flexible&quot;, the official was quoted as saying.</p>
<p>Warships are flexible in operation and can travel the seas freely.</p>
<p>2. flexibility /ˌfleksəˈbɪləti/ (n): tính dẻo, tính mềm dẻo, tính dễ uốn nắn, tính dễ sai bảo, tính linh hoạt, tính linh động # inflexibility /ɪnˌfleksəˈbɪləti/ (n): tính không uốn được, tính không bẻ cong được, tính cứng</p>
<p>The new system offers a much greater degree of flexibility in the way work is organized.</p>
<p>His stubborn inflexibility is unacceptable.</p>
<p>The inflexibility of educational systems makes it difficult to change schools or universities in mid-year.</p>
<p>3. flexibly /ˈfleksəbli/ (adv): linh hoạt # inflexibly /ɪnˈfleksəbli/ (adv): không linh hoạt</p>
<p>An overdraft provides increased flexibility but at a higher cost.</p>
<p>flexibly</p>
<p>4.inflexible /ɪnˈfleksəbl/ (adj): không uốn được, không bẻ cong được, cứng, không nhân nhượng</p>
<p>The prime minister has adopted an inflexible position on immigration.</p>
<p>This type of computer is too slow and inflexible to meet many business needs.</p>
<p>5. destroy (v) /dɪˈstrɔɪ/: phá hủy</p>
<p>These guns will destroy or disable any incoming missile.</p>
<p>Many important historical documents were destroyed in the fire.</p>
<p>In 1906 an earthquake destroyed much of San Francisco.</p>
<p>A bomb fell on the church and destroyed it.</p>
<p>6. destruction /dɪˈstrʌkʃn/ (n): sự phá hủy</p>

<p>Unusually high winds left a trail of destruction over the area.</p>
<p>7. destructive /dɪˈstrʌktɪv/ (adj): phá hủy</p>

<p>The war demonstrated the destructive power of modern weapons.</p>
<p>Opencast coal mining is among the most environmentally destructive activities carried out in Wales.</p>
<p>8. destructible /dɪˈstrʌktəbl/ (adj): có thể phá hủy, có thể mất hiệu lực</p>

"<p>1. locate (v) /ˈləʊkeɪt /: xác định, nằm ở</p>

<p>2. location (n) /ləʊˈkeɪʃn/: vị trí</p>
<p>The hotel is in a beautiful location overlooking the lake.</p>
<p>A map showing the location of the property will be sent to you.</p>
<p>3. locator (n) /ˈləʊkeɪtər/: máy định vị</p>
<p>Satellite locators will keep track of where the trucks are.</p>
<p>This particular sat nav is not a very good speed camera locator.</p>
<p>4. locative (adj) /ˈlɑːkətɪv/: định vị</p>
<p>You seem to ignore the object of that locative phrase.</p>
<p>Locative adverbs do not behave like locative past participles.</p>
<p>5. establish (v) /ɪˈstæblɪʃ/: lập, thành lập</p>
<p>The brewery was established in 1822.</p>
<p>These methods of working were established in the last century.</p>
<p>6. establishment (n) /ɪˈstæblɪʃmənt /: sự thành lập</p>
<p>She seems to have spent all her life studying in educational establishments.</p>
<p>For an inexpensive place to stay, the guide book recommends a small family-run establishment near the cathedral.</p>
<p>They embarked on a tour of the city's many drinking establishments</p>
<p>7. established (adj) /ɪˈstæblɪʃt /: thành lập, sự chứng thật</p>
<p>There are established procedures for dealing with emergencies.</p>
<p>The band doesn't make much money - it's just getting established.</p>
<p>8. dependent (adj) /dɪˈpendənt, əˈpɑːn/: phụ thuộc vào</p>
<p>Most children remain dependent on their parents while at university.</p>
<p>The number of single-parent families dependent on the state has risen enormously in recent years.</p>
<p>He is dependent on his father for support.</p>
<p>He's still financially dependent on his parents.</p>
<p>9. dependable (adj) /dɪˈpendəbl/: đáng tin cậy</p>
<p>I need someone dependable to take care of the children while I'm at work.</p>
<p>I need a dependable baby-sitter</p>
<p>10. depend (v) /dɪˈpend /: phụ thuộc</p>
<p>Whether or not we go to Mexico for our holiday depends on the cost.</p>
<p>I might go to the cinema tomorrow - it depends what time I get home from work.</p>
<p>11. dependent (n) dɪˈpendənt /: phụ thuộc, lệ thuộc, nghiện</p>
<p>My pension will provide for my dependants.</p>
<p>12. dependency (n) /dɪˈpendənsi/: sự phụ thuộc</p>
<p>Their aim is to reduce people's dependency on the welfare state.</p>
<p>13. dependance (n) /dɪˈpendəns/: sự phụ thuộc</p>
<p>The region's complete dependence on tourism is rather worrying.</p>
<p>All her life she had a childlike dependence on the people around her.</p>
<p>Gradually her dependence on alcohol became obvious to everyone.</p>
<p>14. dependability (n) /dɪˌpendəˈbɪləti/: đáng tin cậy</p>
<p>The car offers value for money, comfort, and dependability.</p>
<p>Thomas' teammates appreciated his dependability.</p>
<p>15. survival (n) /sərˈvaɪvl/: sự sống sót, tồn tại</p>
<p>The doctors told my wife I had a 50/50 chance of survival.</p>
<p>His main concern is to ensure his own political survival.</p>
<p>England are fighting for survival (= trying not to be defeated) in this game.</p>
<p>16. survive (v) /sərˈvaɪv/: tồn tại</p>
<p>She was the last surviving member of the family.</p>
<p>Of the six people injured in the crash, only two survived.</p>
<p>Many of these teachers are struggling to survive financially.</p>
<p>17. survivor (n) /sərˈvaɪvər/: người sống sót</p>
<p>One survivor described his torturers as devils incarnate.</p>
<p>The sole survivor of the accident was found in the water after six hours.</p>
<p>A ceasefire has been called to allow the survivors to bury their dead.</p>
<p>The earthquake survivors are in desperate need of help.</p>
<p>18. survivable (adj) /sərˈvaɪvəbl/: có thể sống sót</p>
<p>Between 1969 and 1978 there were 16 survivable crashes, in which 419 people died.</p>
<p>19. survivalism (n) /sərˈvaɪvəlɪzəm/: chủ nghĩa sinh tồn</p>
<p>For him, survivalism started as a hobby and became a way of life.</p>
<p>20. survivalist (n) /sərˈvaɪvəlɪst /: người theo chủ nghĩa sinh tồn</p>
<p>The film-maker goes in search of the weird and wonderful universe of survivalists, flat-earthers, and end-of-the-world prophets.</p>
<p>Many people think of a survivalist as an armed loner with extreme views, but there are many more in America who are simply involved in preparing for lean times, or disaster.</p>
<p>21. orphanage (n) /ˈɔːrfənɪdʒ/: trại mồ côi</p>
<p>From 1950 to 1954, about 400 to 500 children were adopted from this orphanage by domestic families.(Cambridge English Corpus)</p>
<p>Table 3 shows for a few selected subcategories the proportions who were admitted to one of the orphanage</p>
<p>22. orphan (n) /ˈɔːrfn/: mồ côi </p>
<p>The civil war is making orphans of many children.</p>
<p>22. abandon (v) /əˈbændən/: bỏ rơi, từ bỏ</p>
<p>We had to abandon the car.</p>
<p>By the time the rebel troops arrived, the village had already been abandoned.</p>
<p>As a baby he was abandoned by his mother.</p>
<p>We were sinking fast, and the captain gave the order to abandon ship</p>
<p>23. abandonment (n) /əˈbændənmənt /: sự bỏ rơi</p>
<p>The abandonment of the island followed nuclear tests in the area.</p>
<p>His abandonment by his mother when he was a baby affected him all his life.</p>
<p>24. wilderness (n) /ˈwɪldərnəs/: vùng hoang vu.</p>
<p>He abided in the wilderness for forty days.</p>
<p>The area is a trackless wilderness.</p>
<p>If he fails to gain the title, it could mean months in the wilderness.</p>
<p>The area has reverted to wilderness since the mine closed down</p>
<p>25. wild (adj) /waɪld /: hoang dã</p>
<p>The audience burst into wild applause.</p>
<p>When I told him what I'd done, he went wild (= became very angry).</p>
<p>The children were wild with excitement (= were extremely excited).</p>
<p>26. wildly (adv) /ˈwaɪldli/: ngông cuồng</p>
<p>Her weight fluctuates wildly.</p>
<p>There was a man outside the window gesticulating wildly.</p>
<p>Their estimate of the cost of the project was wildly inaccurate.</p>
<p>The children were wildly excited.</p>
<p>27. wildlife (n) /ˈwaɪldlaɪf/: động vật hoang dã</p>
<p>At the museum there was a diorama of local wildlife.</p>
<p>She left a large sum of money in her will to found a wildlife sanctuary.</p>
<p>The use of pesticides is killing off birds, fish and wildlife.</p>
<p>Their work involves restoring and recreating wildlife habitats all across the country</p>
<p>28. recognize (v) /ˈrekəɡnaɪz/: nhận ra</p>
<p>I hadn't seen her for 20 years, but I recognized her immediately.</p>
<p>Do you recognize this song?</p>
<p>Doctors are trained to recognize the symptoms of different diseases.</p>
<p>29. recognition (n) /ˌrekəɡˈnɪʃn/: sự công nhận, sự thừa nhận; sự được công nhận, sự được thừa nhận</p>
<p>It's a new country, hoping for diplomatic recognition from the international community.</p>
<p>There's a growing recognition that this country can no longer afford to be a nuclear power.</p>
<p>30. recognizable (adj) /ˈrekəɡnaɪzəbl/: có thể công nhận, có thể thừa nhận</p>
<p>có thể nhận ra, có thể nhận diện</p>
<p>The Eiffel Tower in Paris is an instantly recognizable landmark.</p>
<p>31. recognizance (n) /rɪˈkɑːɡnɪzəns/: (pháp lý) sự cam kết trước toà (không phá rối trị an; trả nợ...), tiền bảo chứng (cho việc cam kết)</p>
<p>32. recognizably (adv) /ˈrekəɡnaɪzəbli/: dễ nhận biết</p>
<p>The creature was recognizably human.</p>
<p>The setting for the play is recognizably New York.</p>"

<p>59. intention (n) /ɪnˈtenʃn/: ý định, chủ đích</p>

<p>62. suit (v) /ˈsu:t /: thích hợp</p>
