"<p>1. locate (v) /ˈləʊkeɪt /: xác định, nằm ở</p>
<p>The pharmacy is located within the hospital.</p>
<p>The school is located near the river.</p>
<p>The houses will be located on the outskirts of town.</p>
<p>The palace was located in the middle of a forest.</p>
<p>The factory was located too close to a residential area.</p>
<p>2. location (n) /ləʊˈkeɪʃn/: vị trí</p>
<p>The hotel is in a beautiful location overlooking the lake.</p>
<p>A map showing the location of the property will be sent to you.</p>
<p>3. locator (n) /ˈləʊkeɪtər/: máy định vị</p>
<p>Satellite locators will keep track of where the trucks are.</p>
<p>This particular sat nav is not a very good speed camera locator.</p>
<p>4. locative (adj) /ˈlɑːkətɪv/: định vị</p>
<p>You seem to ignore the object of that locative phrase.</p>
<p>Locative adverbs do not behave like locative past participles.</p>
<p>5. establish (v) /ɪˈstæblɪʃ/: lập, thành lập</p>
<p>The brewery was established in 1822.</p>
<p>These methods of working were established in the last century.</p>
<p>6. establishment (n) /ɪˈstæblɪʃmənt /: sự thành lập</p>
<p>She seems to have spent all her life studying in educational establishments.</p>
<p>For an inexpensive place to stay, the guide book recommends a small family-run establishment near the cathedral.</p>
<p>They embarked on a tour of the city's many drinking establishments</p>
<p>7. established (adj) /ɪˈstæblɪʃt /: thành lập, sự chứng thật</p>
<p>There are established procedures for dealing with emergencies.</p>
<p>The band doesn't make much money - it's just getting established.</p>
<p>8. dependent (adj) /dɪˈpendənt, əˈpɑːn/: phụ thuộc vào</p>
<p>Most children remain dependent on their parents while at university.</p>
<p>The number of single-parent families dependent on the state has risen enormously in recent years.</p>
<p>He is dependent on his father for support.</p>
<p>He's still financially dependent on his parents.</p>
<p>9. dependable (adj) /dɪˈpendəbl/: đáng tin cậy</p>
<p>I need someone dependable to take care of the children while I'm at work.</p>
<p>I need a dependable baby-sitter</p>
<p>10. depend (v) /dɪˈpend /: phụ thuộc</p>
<p>Whether or not we go to Mexico for our holiday depends on the cost.</p>
<p>I might go to the cinema tomorrow - it depends what time I get home from work.</p>
<p>11. dependant (n) dɪˈpendənt /: người bảo hộ</p>
<p>My pension will provide for my dependants.</p>
<p>12. dependancy (n) /dɪˈpendənsi/: sự phụ thuộc</p>
<p>Their aim is to reduce people's dependency on the welfare state.</p>

<p>The setting for the play is recognizably New York.</p>
<p>33. habit (n) /ˈhæbɪt /: thói quen</p>
<p>I always buy the same brand of toothpaste out of (= because of) habit.</p>
<p>I'm trying not to get into (= start) the habit of always having biscuits with my coffee.</p>
<p>I used to swim twice a week, but I seem to have got out of (= ended) the habit recently.</p>
<p>I was taught to drive by my boyfriend and I'm afraid I've picked up (= caught) some of his bad habits.</p>
<p>I'm trying to get him to break (= end intentionally) the habit of switching on the TV when he comes home at night.</p>
<p>34. habitat (n) /ˈhæbɪtæt /: môi trường sống, chỗ ở, chỗ cư trú</p>
<p>With so many areas of woodland being cut down, a lot of wildlife is losing its natural habitat.</p>
<p>35. habitable (adj) /ˈhæbɪtəbl/: có thể ở được</p>
<p> lot of improvements would have to be made before the building was habitable.</p>
<p>Some areas of the country are just too cold to be habitable</p>
<p>36. habitation (n) /ˌhæbɪˈteɪʃn/: sự ở, nhà ở, sự cư trú</p>
<p>Wilderness areas are not intended for human habitation.</p>
<p>37. habitual (adj) /həˈbɪtʃuəl/: thói quen, như thường lệ</p>
<p>Longer prison sentences will help keep habitual criminals off the streets</p>

<p>There is something wrong with anyone who is so habitually rude.</p>
<p>There were schools where more than half the students were habitually late.</p>
<p>39. habituated (adj) /həˈbɪtʃueɪtɪd /: có thói quen</p>
<p>We find children's emotional needs difficult to respond to because we are habituated to disregarding our own.</p>

<p>Preheat the oven to a temperature of 200 degrees Celsius.</p>
<p>Temperatures have risen over the past few days (= the weather has become warmer).</p>
<p>The doctor examined him and took his temperature (= measured it).</p>

<p>(Cambridge English Corpus)</p>
<p>There is no reason to assume that disorganized attachment is the consequence of the infant's difficult temperament.</p>

<p>58. intended (adj) /ɪnˈtendɪd /: được dự định; mong đợi # unintended (adj): /ˌʌnɪnˈtendɪd /: không được định hướng trước, không do dự tính trước</p>

<p>60. intentional (adj) /ɪnˈtenʃənl/: cố ý  # unintentional (adj) /ˌʌnɪnˈtenʃənl/: vô ý</p>

"<p>1. locate (v) /ˈləʊkeɪt /: xác định, nằm ở</p>
<p>The pharmacy is located within the hospital.</p>
<p>The school is located near the river.</p>
<p>The houses will be located on the outskirts of town.</p>
<p>The palace was located in the middle of a forest.</p>
<p>The factory was located too close to a residential area.</p>
<p>2. location (n) /ləʊˈkeɪʃn/: vị trí</p>
<p>The hotel is in a beautiful location overlooking the lake.</p>
<p>A map showing the location of the property will be sent to you.</p>
<p>3. locator (n) /ˈləʊkeɪtər/: máy định vị</p>
<p>Satellite locators will keep track of where the trucks are.</p>
<p>This particular sat nav is not a very good speed camera locator.</p>
<p>4. locative (adj) /ˈlɑːkətɪv/: định vị</p>
<p>You seem to ignore the object of that locative phrase.</p>
<p>Locative adverbs do not behave like locative past participles.</p>
<p>5. establish (v) /ɪˈstæblɪʃ/: lập, thành lập</p>
<p>The brewery was established in 1822.</p>
<p>These methods of working were established in the last century.</p>
<p>6. establishment (n) /ɪˈstæblɪʃmənt /: sự thành lập</p>
<p>She seems to have spent all her life studying in educational establishments.</p>
<p>For an inexpensive place to stay, the guide book recommends a small family-run establishment near the cathedral.</p>
<p>They embarked on a tour of the city's many drinking establishments</p>
<p>7. established (adj) /ɪˈstæblɪʃt /: thành lập, sự chứng thật</p>
<p>There are established procedures for dealing with emergencies.</p>
<p>The band doesn't make much money - it's just getting established.</p>
<p>8. dependent (adj) /dɪˈpendənt, əˈpɑːn/: phụ thuộc vào</p>
<p>Most children remain dependent on their parents while at university.</p>
<p>The number of single-parent families dependent on the state has risen enormously in recent years.</p>
<p>He is dependent on his father for support.</p>
<p>He's still financially dependent on his parents.</p>
<p>9. dependable (adj) /dɪˈpendəbl/: đáng tin cậy</p>
<p>I need someone dependable to take care of the children while I'm at work.</p>
<p>I need a dependable baby-sitter</p>

"<p>1. serious (adj) /ˈsɪriəs/: nghiêm túc, đứng đắn, bác học</p>
<p>There were no reports of serious injuries.</p>
<p>The new tax regulations have landed some of the smaller companies in serious trouble.</p>
<p>Drugs have become a serious problem in a lot of schools.</p>
<p>This is a very serious offence.</p>
<p>2. seriously (adv) /ˈsɪriəsli/: nghiêm túc</p>
<p>I seriously think she'll go crazy if she doesn't have a holiday soon.</p>
<p>I would seriously consider moving if I had a child.</p>
<p>Are you seriously telling me that you think you're fat?</p>
<p>No but seriously, I wouldn't worry about that if I were you.</p>
<p>She isn't seriously thinking of telling him, is she?</p>
<p>3. seriousness (n) /ˈsɪriəsnəs/: nghiêm trọng, đứng đắn</p>
<p>I don't think he has any idea of the seriousness of the situation.</p>
<p>I don’t think he has any idea of the seriousness of the situation.</p>
<p>4. emotion (n) /ɪˈməʊʃn/: cảm xúc</p>

<p>5. emotional (adj) /ɪˈməʊʃənl/: đa cảm</p>

<p>6. emotionally (adv) /ɪˈməʊʃənəli/: tình cảm</p>

<p>7. emotionless (adj) /ɪˈməʊʃənləs/: vô cảm</p>

<p>8. especially (adv) /ɪˈspeʃəli/: đặc biệt là</p>

<p>Rather, they will be understood as integrally constructive of the picture itself.</p>

<p>20. solemnity (n) /səˈlemnəti/: trang trọng, nghi thức</p>
<p>I do not desire to read it now, but the ceremony of naturalisation goes through in this country with all sorts of solemnities.</p>
<p>21. solemnly (v) /ˈsɑːləmli/: trọng thể; chính thức long trọng; trang nghiêm uy nghi, uy nghiêm</p>
<p>&quot;I saw things I hope to never see again,&quot; she said solemnly.</p>
<p>He solemnly declares that he has made up his mind to become a priest.</p>
<p>The opposition leaders solemnly pledged to co-operate with the prime minister.</p>
<p>22. mournful (adj) /ˈmɔːrnfl/: tang thương</p>
<p>We sang the music; the canon was excellent and very mournful.</p>
<p>23. mourner (n) /ˈmɔːrnər/: người đưa tang</p>
<p>The dead man's wife and children were the chief mourners.</p>
<p>24. mournfully (adv) /ˈmɔːrnfəli/: thê lương</p>
<p>He gazed mournfully out the window.</p>
<p>The church's funeral bell tolled mournfully over the neighbourhood.</p>
<p>25. mourn (v) /mɔːrn/: thương tiếc</p>
<p>Queen Victoria mourned Prince Albert /Prince Albert's death for 40 years.</p>
<p>She was still mourning for her brother.</p>
<p>They mourned the passing of an older, simpler way of life.</p>"

"<p>1. serious (adj) /ˈsɪriəs/: nghiêm túc, đứng đắn, bác học</p>
<p>There were no reports of serious injuries.</p>
<p>The new tax regulations have landed some of the smaller companies in serious trouble.</p>
<p>Drugs have become a serious problem in a lot of schools.</p>
<p>This is a very serious offence.</p>
<p>2. seriously (adv) /ˈsɪriəsli/: nghiêm túc</p>
<p>I seriously think she'll go crazy if she doesn't have a holiday soon.</p>
<p>I would seriously consider moving if I had a child.</p>
<p>Are you seriously telling me that you think you're fat?</p>
<p>No but seriously, I wouldn't worry about that if I were you.</p>
<p>She isn't seriously thinking of telling him, is she?</p>
<p>3. seriousness (n) /ˈsɪriəsnəs/: nghiêm trọng, đứng đắn</p>
<p>I don't think he has any idea of the seriousness of the situation.</p>
<p>I don’t think he has any idea of the seriousness of the situation.</p>
<p>4. emotion (n) /ɪˈməʊʃn/: cảm xúc</p>
<p>He showed no emotion as he walked into the witness box.</p>
<p>Overcome by emotion, she found herself unable to speak for a few minutes.</p>
<p>5. emotional (adj) /ɪˈməʊʃənl/: đa cảm</p>
<p>He's a very emotional man.</p>
<p>I felt quite emotional during the wedding ceremony.</p>
<p>He became very emotional when I told him I was pregnant.</p>
<p>The president has made an emotional plea for the killing to stop.</p>
<p>6. emotionally (adv) /ɪˈməʊʃənəli/: tình cảm</p>
<p>Many children have become emotionally disturbed as a result of the abuse they have ssuffererd.</p>
<p>He was not an emotionally stable person.</p>
<p>7. emotionless (adj) /ɪˈməʊʃənləs/: vô cảm</p>
<p>To your right is a moustachioed man in an upright chair, his face emotionless as he looks straight out at yo</p>
<p>8. especially (adv) /ɪˈspeʃəli/: đặc biệt là</p>
<p>She's not especially interested in sport.</p>
<p>I love Australian wines, especially the white wines.</p>
<p>9. especial (adj) /ɪˈspeʃl/: đặc biệt</p>
<p>My especial commendation of the book responds to a matter which is more basic and too often neglected.</p>
<p>10. integral (adj) /ˈɪntɪɡrəl/: gắn liền</p>
<p>He's an integral part of the team and we can't do without him.</p>
<p>Bars and terrace cafés are integral to the social life of the city.</p>
<p>11. integrally (adv) /ˈɪntɪɡrəli/: giữa các chủng tộc</p>
<p>The second, integrally related to the first, is correction of error made by lower-order processes. (Cambridge English Corpus )</p>
<p>Rather, they will be understood as integrally constructive of the picture itself.</p>
<p>12. integrate (v) /ˈɪntɪɡreɪt /: tích hợp</p>
<p>He seems to find it difficult to integrate socially.</p>
<p>It's very difficult to integrate yourself into a society whose culture is so different from your own.</p>
<p>Children are often very good at integrating into a new culture.</p>
<p>13. joy (n) /dʒɔɪ/: vui sướng, niềm vui</p>
<p>Her books have brought joy to millions.</p>
<p>14. joyfully (adv) /ˈdʒɔɪfəli/: vui mừng</p>
<p>They lived life simply, joyfully and dedicated to their children.</p>
<p>She passed the finishing line joyfully.</p>
<p>15. joyless (adj) /ˈdʒɔɪləs/: không vui, buồn</p>
<p>Jane is trapped in a joyless marriage.</p>
<p>16. funeral (n) /ˈfjuːnərəl: đám tang</p>
<p>The funeral will be held next Friday.</p>
<p>Over 300 mourners attended the funeral.</p>
<p>17. funereal (adj) /fjuˈnɪriəl/: thích hợp với đám ma buồn thảm (như) khi đi đưa đám</p>
<p>It has been rather a tedious and sometimes a funereal business.</p>
<p>18. solemn (adj) /ˈsɑːləm/: trang nghiêm</p>
<p>He looked stern and solemn, and rarely spoke.</p>
<p>The memorial was a very solemn occasion.</p>

<p>Her books are always entertaining and this one is no exception.</p>
<p>It's a very entertaining play with a hilarious final act.</p>
<p>His books are just silly nonsense but they're entertaining, I suppose.</p>
<p>32. entertainingly (adv) /ˌentərˈteɪnɪŋli/: hấp dẫn, thú vị giải trí</p>

<p>The play was skilfully and entertainingly acted.</p>

<p>With uplifted arms, he ran towards them.</p>

<p>For me it was a marvellously uplifting performance.</p>
<p>36. criticize (v) /ˈkrɪtɪsaɪz/: chỉ trích</p>
<p>The government is being widely criticized in the media for failing to limit air pollution.</p>
<p>We'll get nowhere if all you can do is criticize.</p>
<p>37. criticism (n) /ˈkrɪtɪsɪzəm/: sự phê bình, sự phê phán, sự bình phẩm, sự chỉ trích</p>

<p>44. composed (adj) /kəmˈpəʊzd /: bình tĩnh, điềm tĩnh</p>
<p>She looked remarkably composed throughout the funeral.</p>
<p>45. lyrical (adj) /ˈlɪrɪkl/: trữ tình</p>
<p>The book contains lyrical descriptions of the author's childhood.</p>
<p>46. lyric (n) /ˈlɪrɪk/: lời bài hát</p>
<p>Paul Simon writes the lyrics for most of his songs.</p>
<p>47. lyrically (adv) /ˈlɪrɪkli/: trữ tình</p>
<p>The place is lyrically named Strawberry Canyon.</p>
<p>It is a wistful tale told in verse and lyrically illustrated.</p>
<p>She is a lyrically adventurous songwriter.</p>

<p>The harshness of the book's subject is softened by a certain lyricism in the writing.</p>

<p>The language style of a song depends on its lyricist.</p>
<p>50. except (v) /ɪkˈsept / for:  trừ, chỉ trừ</p>
<p>We work every day except Sunday.</p>
<p>They all came except Matt.</p>
<p>I had nothing on except for my socks.</p>
<p>51. exception (n) /ɪkˈsepʃn/: loại bỏ ra hoặc không kể đến; người hoặc vật không được tính vào; ngoại lệ; biệt lệ</p>
<p>Men are usually quite good at map-reading but Tim is the exception.</p>
<p>There are exceptions to every rule.</p>
<p>I like all kinds of movies with the exception of (= but not) horror movies.</p>
<p>Her books are always entertaining and this one is no exception.</p>
<p>You must report here every Tuesday without exception.</p>
<p>52. exceptional (adj) /ɪkˈsepʃənl/: đặc biệt, phi thường</p>
<p>The company has shown exceptional growth over the past two years.</p>
<p>53. exceptionally (adv) /ɪkˈsepʃənəli/: cá biệt, khác thường</p>
<p>The school is for exceptionally gifted musicians.</p>
<p>The event has been exceptionally well attended.</p>
<p>It's unclear whether he knew about the exceptionally high lead levels in the house.</p>"

<p>46. lyric (n) /ˈlɪrɪk/: lời bài hát</p>

<p>51. exception (n) /ɪkˈsepʃn/: loại bỏ ra hoặc không kể đến; người hoặc vật không được tính vào; ngoại lệ; biệt lệ</p>

<p>55. appropriately (adv) /əˈprəʊpriətli/: thích hợp, thích đáng</p>
<p>56. appropriateness (n) /əˈprəʊpriətnəs/: sự phù hợp</p>
<p>57. artistic (adj) /ɑːrˈtɪstɪk/: mang tính chất nghệ thuật</p>
<p>58. art (n) /ɑːrt /: mỹ thuật, nghệ thuật</p>
<p>59. appreciate (v) /əˈpriːʃieɪt /: coi trọng, đánh giá cao</p>

<p>61. appreciably (adv) /əˈpriːʃəbli/: đáng kể, thấy rõ</p>
<p>62. appreciation (n) /əˌpriːʃiˈeɪʃn/: sự đánh giá</p>

<p>69. popular (adj) /ˈpɑːpjələr/: được nhiều người ưa chuộng, được nhiều người ngưỡng mộ, được nhiều người ưa thích; phổ biến, nổi tiếng</p>
<p>70. popularize (v) /ˈpɑːpjələraɪz/: đại chúng hoá truyền bá, phổ cập; phổ biến</p>
<p>71. popularity (n) /ˌpɑːpjuˈlærəti/: tính đại chúng; tính phổ biến</p>
<p>72. popularization (n) /ˌpɑːpjələrəˈzeɪʃn/: sự đại chúng hoá, sự truyền bá, sự phổ cập; sự phổ biến</p>
<p>73. populate (v) /ˈpɑːpjuleɪt /: ở, trú ngụ</p>
<p>74. popularly (adv) /ˈpɑːpjələrli/: được quần chúng ưa thích, được nhân dân yêu mến</p>"
"<p>1. serious (adj) /ˈsɪriəs/: nghiêm túc, đứng đắn, bác học</p>
<p>There were no reports of serious injuries.</p>
<p>The new tax regulations have landed some of the smaller companies in serious trouble.</p>
<p>Drugs have become a serious problem in a lot of schools.</p>
<p>This is a very serious offence.</p>
<p>2. seriously (adv) /ˈsɪriəsli/: nghiêm túc</p>
<p>I seriously think she'll go crazy if she doesn't have a holiday soon.</p>
<p>I would seriously consider moving if I had a child.</p>
<p>Are you seriously telling me that you think you're fat?</p>
<p>No but seriously, I wouldn't worry about that if I were you.</p>
<p>She isn't seriously thinking of telling him, is she?</p>
<p>3. seriousness (n) /ˈsɪriəsnəs/: nghiêm trọng, đứng đắn</p>
<p>I don't think he has any idea of the seriousness of the situation.</p>
<p>I don’t think he has any idea of the seriousness of the situation.</p>
<p>4. emotion (n) /ɪˈməʊʃn/: cảm xúc</p>
<p>He showed no emotion as he walked into the witness box.</p>
<p>Overcome by emotion, she found herself unable to speak for a few minutes.</p>
<p>5. emotional (adj) /ɪˈməʊʃənl/: đa cảm</p>
<p>He's a very emotional man.</p>
<p>I felt quite emotional during the wedding ceremony.</p>
<p>He became very emotional when I told him I was pregnant.</p>
<p>The president has made an emotional plea for the killing to stop.</p>
<p>6. emotionally (adv) /ɪˈməʊʃənəli/: tình cảm</p>
<p>Many children have become emotionally disturbed as a result of the abuse they have ssuffererd.</p>
<p>He was not an emotionally stable person.</p>
<p>7. emotionless (adj) /ɪˈməʊʃənləs/: vô cảm</p>
<p>To your right is a moustachioed man in an upright chair, his face emotionless as he looks straight out at yo</p>
<p>8. especially (adv) /ɪˈspeʃəli/: đặc biệt là</p>
<p>She's not especially interested in sport.</p>
<p>I love Australian wines, especially the white wines.</p>
<p>9. especial (adj) /ɪˈspeʃl/: đặc biệt</p>
<p>My especial commendation of the book responds to a matter which is more basic and too often neglected.</p>
<p>10. integral (adj) /ˈɪntɪɡrəl/: gắn liền</p>
<p>He's an integral part of the team and we can't do without him.</p>
<p>Bars and terrace cafés are integral to the social life of the city.</p>
<p>11. integrally (adv) /ˈɪntɪɡrəli/: giữa các chủng tộc</p>
<p>The second, integrally related to the first, is correction of error made by lower-order processes. (Cambridge English Corpus )</p>
<p>Rather, they will be understood as integrally constructive of the picture itself.</p>
<p>12. integrate (v) /ˈɪntɪɡreɪt /: tích hợp</p>
<p>He seems to find it difficult to integrate socially.</p>
<p>It's very difficult to integrate yourself into a society whose culture is so different from your own.</p>
<p>Children are often very good at integrating into a new culture.</p>
<p>13. joy (n) /dʒɔɪ/: vui sướng, niềm vui</p>
<p>Her books have brought joy to millions.</p>
<p>14. joyfully (adv) /ˈdʒɔɪfəli/: vui mừng</p>
<p>They lived life simply, joyfully and dedicated to their children.</p>
<p>She passed the finishing line joyfully.</p>
<p>15. joyless (adj) /ˈdʒɔɪləs/: không vui, buồn</p>
<p>Jane is trapped in a joyless marriage.</p>
<p>16. funeral (n) /ˈfjuːnərəl: đám tang</p>
<p>The funeral will be held next Friday.</p>
<p>Over 300 mourners attended the funeral.</p>
<p>17. funereal (adj) /fjuˈnɪriəl/: thích hợp với đám ma buồn thảm (như) khi đi đưa đám</p>
<p>It has been rather a tedious and sometimes a funereal business.</p>
<p>18. solemn (adj) /ˈsɑːləm/: trang nghiêm</p>
<p>He looked stern and solemn, and rarely spoke.</p>
<p>The memorial was a very solemn occasion.</p>
<p>19. solemnize (v) /ˈsɑːləmnaɪz/: cử hành theo nghi thức (đám cưới..) làm nghiêm, làm cho long trọng</p>
<p>Marriage is solemnized mainly through negotiation.</p>
<p>20. solemnity (n) /səˈlemnəti/: trang trọng, nghi thức</p>
<p>I do not desire to read it now, but the ceremony of naturalisation goes through in this country with all sorts of solemnities.</p>
<p>21. solemnly (v) /ˈsɑːləmli/: trọng thể; chính thức long trọng; trang nghiêm uy nghi, uy nghiêm</p>
<p>&quot;I saw things I hope to never see again,&quot; she said solemnly.</p>
<p>He solemnly declares that he has made up his mind to become a priest.</p>
<p>The opposition leaders solemnly pledged to co-operate with the prime minister.</p>
<p>22. mournful (adj) /ˈmɔːrnfl/: tang thương</p>
<p>We sang the music; the canon was excellent and very mournful.</p>
<p>23. mourner (n) /ˈmɔːrnər/: người đưa tang</p>
<p>The dead man's wife and children were the chief mourners.</p>
<p>24. mournfully (adv) /ˈmɔːrnfəli/: thê lương</p>
<p>He gazed mournfully out the window.</p>
<p>The church's funeral bell tolled mournfully over the neighbourhood.</p>
<p>25. mourn (v) /mɔːrn/: thương tiếc</p>
<p>Queen Victoria mourned Prince Albert /Prince Albert's death for 40 years.</p>
<p>She was still mourning for her brother.</p>
<p>They mourned the passing of an older, simpler way of life.</p>
<p>26. lull (v) /lʌl/: ru ngủ</p>
<p>The motion of the car almost lulled her to sleep.</p>
<p>27. lullaby (n) /ˈlʌləbaɪ/: hát ru</p>
<p>They were also asked about their thoughts on lullaby selections during their final interviews.</p>
<p>28. entertainment (n) /ˌentərˈteɪnmənt / sự giải trí</p>
<p>There's not much in the way of entertainment in this town - just the cinema and a couple of pubs.</p>
<p>This season's entertainments include five new plays and several concerts of Chinese and Indian music.</p>
<p>29. entertain (v) /ˌentərˈteɪn/: sự giải trí</p>
<p>Milligan's anarchic humor has always had the power to offend as well as entertain.</p>
<p>Year after year they wheel out the same third-rate celebrities to entertain us.</p>
<p>Should the function of children's television be to entertain or to enlighten?</p>
<p>The crowd was entertained with a display of aerobatics.</p>
<p>30. entertainer (n) /ˌentərˈteɪnər/: người giải trí</p>
<p>Although her acting skills were limited, she was a great entertainer.</p>
<p>We stopped to watch some street entertainers who were performing in the town square.</p>
<p>The Royal Variety Show is an opportunity to see some of our finest entertainers - comedians, singers, dancers and magicians.</p>
<p>32. entertaining (adj) /ˌentərˈteɪnɪŋ/: giải trí, làm cho vui</p>
<p>She gave a witty, entertaining and articulate speech.</p>
<p>He had gained a reputation as an entertaining speaker.</p>
<p>Her books are always entertaining and this one is no exception.</p>
<p>It's a very entertaining play with a hilarious final act.</p>
<p>His books are just silly nonsense but they're entertaining, I suppose.</p>
<p>32. entertainingly (adv) /ˌentərˈteɪnɪŋli/: hấp dẫn, thú vị giải trí</p>
<p>He spoke his mind freely and entertainingly.</p>
<p>The play was skilfully and entertainingly acted.</p>
<p>33. uplift (adj) /ˈʌplɪft /: hưng phấn, bay bổng</p>
<p>The wings are designed to provide uplift when the plane is flying horizontally.</p>
<p>34. uplifted (adj) /ˌʌpˈlɪftɪd /: thăng hoa, vui sướng</p>
<p>With uplifted arms, he ran towards them.</p>
<p>35. uplifting (adj) /ˌʌpˈlɪftɪŋ/: nâng cao tinh thần</p>
<p>For me it was a marvellously uplifting performance.</p>
<p>36. criticize (v) /ˈkrɪtɪsaɪz/: chỉ trích</p>
<p>The government is being widely criticized in the media for failing to limit air pollution.</p>
<p>We'll get nowhere if all you can do is criticize.</p>
<p>37. criticism (n) /ˈkrɪtɪsɪzəm/: sự phê bình, sự phê phán, sự bình phẩm, sự chỉ trích</p>
<p>Her lack of interest in the project has provoked sharp criticism from colleagues.</p>
<p>You must learn not to overreact to criticism.</p>
<p>The government is currently facing severe criticism.</p>
<p>I think he felt discouraged because of all the criticism he'd received.</p>
<p>38. serene (adj) /səˈriːn/: thanh bình, tĩnh lặng</p>
<p>She has a lovely serene face.</p>
<p>39. serendipity (n) /ˌserənˈdɪpəti/: sự tình cờ</p>
<p>We should not forget, though, that serendipity has yielded some of our most important agents.</p>
<p>40. serenely (adv) /səˈriːnli/: thanh thản</p>
<p>She smiled serenely and said nothing.</p>
<p>&quot;It is really quite easy,&quot; he said serenely.</p>
<p>Xem</p>
<p>41. serenity (n) /səˈrenəti/: thanh thản, êm đềm</p>
<p>I admired her serenity in the midst of so much chaos.</p>
<p>The hotel offers a tranquil haven of peace and serenity, away from the bustle of the city.</p>
<p>Xem</p>
<p>42. compose (v) /kəmˈpəʊz/: sọan nhạc, sáng tác nhạc</p>
<p>The music was specially composed for the film.</p>
<p>43. composer (n) /kəmˈpəʊzər/: nhà soạn nhạc</p>
<p>As a composer, he was up there with the best.</p>
<p>In my opinion, no other composers even begin to approach Mozart.</p>
<p>44. composed (adj) /kəmˈpəʊzd /: bình tĩnh, điềm tĩnh</p>
<p>She looked remarkably composed throughout the funeral.</p>
<p>45. lyrical (adj) /ˈlɪrɪkl/: trữ tình</p>
<p>The book contains lyrical descriptions of the author's childhood.</p>
<p>46. lyric (n) /ˈlɪrɪk/: lời bài hát</p>
<p>Paul Simon writes the lyrics for most of his songs.</p>
<p>47. lyrically (adv) /ˈlɪrɪkli/: trữ tình</p>
<p>The place is lyrically named Strawberry Canyon.</p>
<p>It is a wistful tale told in verse and lyrically illustrated.</p>
<p>She is a lyrically adventurous songwriter.</p>
<p>48. lyricism (n) /ˈlɪrɪsɪzəm/: trữ tình</p>
<p>The harshness of the book's subject is softened by a certain lyricism in the writing.</p>
<p>49. lyricist (n) /ˈlɪrɪsɪst /: người viết lời</p>
<p>The language style of a song depends on its lyricist.</p>
<p>50. except (v) /ɪkˈsept / for:  trừ, chỉ trừ</p>
<p>We work every day except Sunday.</p>
<p>They all came except Matt.</p>
<p>I had nothing on except for my socks.</p>
<p>51. exception (n) /ɪkˈsepʃn/: loại bỏ ra hoặc không kể đến; người hoặc vật không được tính vào; ngoại lệ; biệt lệ</p>
<p>Men are usually quite good at map-reading but Tim is the exception.</p>
<p>There are exceptions to every rule.</p>
<p>I like all kinds of movies with the exception of (= but not) horror movies.</p>
<p>Her books are always entertaining and this one is no exception.</p>
<p>You must report here every Tuesday without exception.</p>
<p>52. exceptional (adj) /ɪkˈsepʃənl/: đặc biệt, phi thường</p>
<p>The company has shown exceptional growth over the past two years.</p>
<p>53. exceptionally (adv) /ɪkˈsepʃənəli/: cá biệt, khác thường</p>
<p>The school is for exceptionally gifted musicians.</p>
<p>The event has been exceptionally well attended.</p>
<p>It's unclear whether he knew about the exceptionally high lead levels in the house.</p>
<p>54. appropriate (adj) /əˈprəʊpriət /: thích hợp, thích đáng</p>
<p>I didn't think his comments were very appropriate at the time.</p>
<p>Is this an appropriate occasion to discuss finance?</p>
<p>Please complete the appropriate parts of this form (= the parts that are right or necessary for your particular situation) and return it as soon as possible.</p>
<p>55. appropriately (adv) /əˈprəʊpriətli/: thích hợp, thích đáng</p>
<p>She didn't think we were appropriately dressed for a wedding.</p>
<p>Business leaders who acted appropriately were widely praised.</p>
<p>56. appropriateness (n) /əˈprəʊpriətnəs/: sự phù hợp</p>
<p>People disagree about the appropriateness of public funding.</p>
<p>Some of the books were longer and he questioned their appropriateness for five-year-olds.</p>
<p>She didn't think we were appropriately dressed for a wedding.</p>
<p>Business leaders who acted appropriately were widely praised.</p>
<p>57. artistic (adj) /ɑːrˈtɪstɪk/: mang tính chất nghệ thuật</p>
<p>That's a very artistic flower arrangement you have there.</p>
<p>58. art (n) /ɑːrt /: mỹ thuật, nghệ thuật</p>
<p>Can television and pop music really be considered art?</p>
<p>I enjoyed the ballet, but it wasn't really great art.</p>
<p>59. appreciate (v) /əˈpriːʃieɪt /: coi trọng, đánh giá cao</p>
<p>There's no point buying him expensive wines - he doesn't appreciate them.</p>
<p>60. appreciable (adj) /əˈpriːʃəbl/: có thể đánh giá được thấy rõ được, đáng kể</p>
<p>There has been an appreciable drop in the number of unemployed since the new government came to power.</p>
<p>61. appreciably (adv) /əˈpriːʃəbli/: đáng kể, thấy rõ</p>
<p>Her health has improved appreciably since she changed her treatment.</p>
<p>At 60, I find I now have appreciably less hair.</p>
<p>62. appreciation (n) /əˌpriːʃiˈeɪʃn/: sự đánh giá</p>
<p>Max has no appreciation of the finer things in life.</p>
<p>The crowd cheered in appreciation.</p>
<p>Children rarely show any appreciation of/for what their parents do for them.</p>
<p>These flowers are a token of my appreciation of/for all your help.</p>
<p>63. appreciative (adj) /əˈpriːʃətɪv/: đánh giá cao, khen ngợi</p>
<p>t's nice to have an appreciative audience.</p>
<p>I'm very appreciative of all the support you've given me.</p>
<p>64. appreciatively (adv) /əˈpriːʃətɪvli/: khen ngợi, tán dương, tán thưởng</p>
<p>She smiled appreciatively at him.</p>
<p>The crowd laughed appreciatively.</p>
<p>65. cheer /tʃɪr/ (v) somebody up: làm ai cảm thấy vui vẻ</p>
<p>Everyone cheered as the winners received their medals.</p>
<p>He was cheering for the other side.</p>
<p>66. cheerful (adj) /ˈtʃɪrfl/: tươi vui</p>
<p>He's usually fairly cheerful.</p>
<p>You're in a cheerful mood this morning.</p>
<p>She manages to stay cheerful (= happy and positive) despite everything.</p>
<p>67. cheerfully (adv) /ˈtʃɪrfəli/: vui vẻ</p>
<p>She walked down the road, whistling cheerfully.</p>
<p>&quot;Hello, Mrs Morris!&quot; he exclaimed cheerfully.</p>
<p>68. cheerfulness (n) /ˈtʃɪrflnəs/: luôn vui vẻ</p>
<p>It's hard not to be affected by her enthusiasm and cheerfulness.</p>
<p>His cheerfulness and modesty was rooted in a happy childhood.</p>
<p>69. popular (adj) /ˈpɑːpjələr/: được nhiều người ưa chuộng, được nhiều người ngưỡng mộ, được nhiều người ưa thích; phổ biến, nổi tiếng</p>
<p>She's the most popular teacher in school.</p>
<p>That song was popular with people from my father's generation.</p>
<p>Walking is a popular form of exercise in Britain.</p>
<p>How popular is Madonna among/with teenagers?</p>
<p>70. popularize (v) /ˈpɑːpjələraɪz/: đại chúng hoá truyền bá, phổ cập; phổ biến</p>
<p>Television has an important role to play in popularizing new scientific ideas.</p>
<p>71. popularity (n) /ˌpɑːpjuˈlærəti/: tính đại chúng; tính phổ biến</p>
<p>The prime minister is riding on a wave of popularity.</p>
<p>Cinema in Britain is undergoing a revival of popularity.</p>
<p>By the late 70s the group's popularity was beginning to wane.</p>
<p>72. popularization (n) /ˌpɑːpjələrəˈzeɪʃn/: sự đại chúng hoá, sự truyền bá, sự phổ cập; sự phổ biến</p>
<p>She wrote a history of the popularization of Chinese food in the USA.</p>
<p>Internet cafes have contributed significantly to the popularization of the internet.</p>

<p>13. violence (n) /ˈvaɪələns/: sự ác liệt, sự dữ dội, sự mãnh liệt; tính ác liệt, tính thô bạo</p>

<p>14. violently (adv) /ˈvaɪələntli/: mãnh liệt, dữ, kịch liệt</p>

<p>The car hit a patch of ice and slewed around violently.</p>
<p>They were violently opposed to change.</p>
<p>15. disgusting (adj) /dɪsˈɡʌstɪŋ/: đáng khinh miệt</p>
<p>It's disgusting that there are no schools or hospitals for these people.</p>
<p>Passengers were kept for three hours in a disgusting waiting room.</p>
<p>16. disgusted (adj) /dɪsˈɡʌstɪd /: chán ghét</p>
<p>She was disgusted at the way they treated their children.</p>
<p>I'm totally disgusted with your behaviour.</p>
<p>17. disgustedly (adv) /dɪsˈɡʌstɪdli/: ghê tởm</p>
<p>He tasted the soup, then shook his head disgustedly.</p>
<p>&quot;They've done absolutely nothing about it,&quot; she said disgustedly.</p>
<p>18. disgustingly (adv) /dɪsˈɡʌstɪŋli/: kinh tởm</p>
<p>These white walls are much better than that disgusting old wallpaper.</p>
<p>The food was absolutely disgusting - I couldn't eat it.</p>
<p>I find some of his habits rather unpleasant, disgusting even.</p>
<p>Stop picking your nose. You really are disgusting.</p>
<p>19. disgust (n) /dɪsˈɡʌst /: làm ghê tởm, làm kinh tởm; làm chán ghét, làm ghét cay ghét đắng làm phẫn nộ, làm căm phẫn</p>
<p>She walked out in disgust.</p>
<p>We are demonstrating to show our anger and disgust at the treatment of refugees.</p>
<p>He resigned from the committee in disgust at the corruption.</p>
<p>20. thriller (n) /ˈθrɪlər/: phim giật gân</p>
<p>It's described here as a taut psychological thriller.</p>
<p>21. thrill (n) /θrɪl/: sự run lên, sự rùng mình; sự chấn động tinh thần (do kinh sợ..)</p>
<p>So why do people still go hunting - is it the thrill of the chase?</p>
<p>It gave me a real thrill to see her again after so many years.</p>
<p>22. thrilling (adj) /ˈθrɪlɪŋ/: làm rùng mình; cảm động, xúc động, hồi hộp, ly kỳ</p>
<p>The book is a thrilling adventure story.</p>
<p>23. thrilled (adj) /θrɪld /: hồi hộp</p>
<p>My parents weren’t too thrilled when they found out.</p>
<p>24. thrillingly (adv) /ˈθrɪlɪŋli/: li kỳ</p>
<p>They are hoping to retain the title so thrillingly won last year.</p>
<p>25. sequence (n) /ˈsi:kwəns/: trình tự, chuỗi</p>
<p>The first chapter describes the strange sequence of events that led to his death.</p>
<p>Is there a particular sequence in which you have to perform these tasks?</p>
<p>26. sequencer (n) /ˈsiːkwənsər/: (tin học) bộ sắp xếp dãy</p>
<p>This year marine scientists did just that—with a portable sequencer the size of a smartphone scientists were able to determine which jellyfish species were in a particular marine habitat with several cups of water.</p>
<p>27. sequencing (n) /ˈsiːkwənsɪŋ/: sự sắp xếp dãy, sự sắp xếp chuỗi, sự sắp xếp thứ tự</p>
<p>A common sign of dyslexia is that the sequencing of letters when spelling words may be incorrect.</p>
<p>28. sequential (adj) /sɪˈkwenʃl/: liên tục, liên tiếp theo sau, tiếp sau (ảnh hưởng...); (toán học) dãy, theo dãytuần tự</p>
<p>The publishers claim that the book constitutes &quot;the first sequential exposition of events and thus of the history of the revolution&quot;.</p>
<p>29. sequentially (adv) sequential : tuần tự, luân phiên</p>
<p>References are numbered sequentially as they appear in the text.</p>
<p>Sales have improved sequentially for four quarters.</p>
<p>He has approached his subject geographically rather than sequentially.</p>"

"<p>1. romantic /rəʊˈmæntɪk/ film (n): phim lãng mạn</p>
<p>His latest film is described as a 'romantic comedy'.</p>
<p>Sing one of those romantic numbers.</p>
<p>She wished her husband was a bit more romantic.</p>
<p>2. romance (n) /ˈrəʊmæns/: không khí lãng mạn; tình cảm lãng mạn</p>
<p>They got married last year after a whirlwind (= very short and unexpected) romance.</p>
<p>It was just a holiday romance.</p>
<p>Office romances are usually a bad idea.</p>
<p>3. silent /ˈsaɪlənt / film (n): phim câm</p>
<p>She whispered a silent prayer that her wounded brother would not die.</p>

<p>4. silently (adv) /ˈsaɪləntli/: thầm lặng</p>

<p>5. vivid (adj) /ˈvɪvɪd /: sống động</p>

<p>6. vividly (adv) /ˈvɪvɪdli/: chói, chói lọi, sặc sỡ (màu sắc, ánh sáng) mạnh mẽ, đầy sức sống; (người) sống động, mạnh mẽ (khả năng trí tuệ)</p>

<p>7. vividness (n) /ˈvɪvɪdnəs/: tính chất chói, tính chất chói lọi, tính chất sặc sỡ (màu sắc, ánh sáng) tính chất mạnh mẽ, tính chất đầy sức sống; (người) tính chất sống động, tính chất mạnh mẽ (khả năng trí tuệ)</p>

"<p>1. champion (n) /ˈtʃæmpiən/: nhà vô địch</p>

<p>The defending champion will play his first match of the tournament tomorrow.</p>

<p>3. consider (v) /kənˈsɪdər/: đánh giá, coi (là)</p>
<p>She's being considered for the job.</p>
<p>I'd like some time to consider before I make a decision.</p>
<p>4. consideration (n) /kənˌsɪdəˈreɪʃn/: sự xem xét</p>
<p>As I was just saying, I think the proposal needs further consideration.</p>
<p>Three sites are presently under consideration for the new hotel.</p>
<p>I've put my proposition to the company director for his consideration.</p>
<p>The proposals that you have put forward deserve serious consideration.</p>
<p>5. considerable (adj) /kənˈsɪdərəbl/: đáng kể</p>
<p>The fire caused considerable damage to the church.</p>
<p>6. considerate (v) /kənˈsɪdərət /: thận trọng, chu đáo, ý tứ</p>
<p>It wasn't very considerate of you to drink all the milk.</p>
<p>Đối lập</p>
<p>7. considerately (adv) /kənˈsɪdərətli/: thận trọng, chu đáo, y tứ</p>
<p>She drives carefully and considerately.</p>
<p>8. considerably (adv) /kənˈsɪdərəbli/: đáng kể</p>
<p>He's considerably fatter than he was when I knew him.</p>
<p>His views differ considerably from those of his parents.</p>
<p>9. passionate (adj) /ˈpæ∫ənət /: say đắm, nồng nàn; nồng nhiệt, thiết tha</p>
<p>The child's mother made a passionate plea for help.</p>
<p>Joe is passionate about baseball (= he likes it very much).</p>
<p>10. passion (n) /ˈpæʃn/: cảm xúc mạnh mẽ, tình cảm nồng nàn</p>
<p>Football arouses a good deal of passion among its fans.</p>

<p>11. passionless (adj) /ˈpæʃnləs/: không sôi nổi, không say sưa, không nồng nàn, không nồng nhiệt, không thiết tha</p>

<p>She is a superstar all around the globe.</p>
<p>14. globalize (v) /ˈɡləʊbəlaɪz/: biến thành toàn cầu, áp dụng cho cả thế giới</p>
<p>Satellite broadcasting is helping to globalize television.</p>
<p>As the economy develops, it will continue to globalize.</p>
<p>15. globalism (n) /ˈɡləʊbəlɪzəm/: chủ nghĩa toàn cầu</p>
<p>There had been hopes that the euro would lead to a golden age of economic globalism.</p>
<p>16. globalist (n) /ˈɡləʊbəlɪst /: người theo chủ nghĩa toàn cầu</p>
<p>He is a globalist, whereas we are nationalists who will put our country first.</p>
<p>She is critical of the president's globalist foreign policy.</p>
<p>17. globalization (n) /ˌɡləʊbələˈzeɪʃn/: toàn cầu hóa</p>
<p>We must take advantage of the increased globalization of the commodity trading business.</p>
<p>18. attract (v) /əˈtrækt /: thu hút</p>
<p>These flowers are brightly coloured in order to attract butterflies.</p>
<p>The circus is attracting huge crowds/audiences.</p>
<p>19. attraction (n) /ˌɡləʊbələˈzeɪʃn/: sự thu hút</p>
<p>Life in Los Angeles has so many attractions - nightclubs, good restaurants, and so on.</p>
<p>tourist attractions</p>
<p>The opportunity to travel is one of the main attractions of this job.</p>
<p>Skiing holds no attraction for me.</p>
<p>20. attractive(adj) /əˈtræktɪv/: thu hút, hấp dẫn # unattractive (adj) /ˌʌnəˈtræktɪv/: không thu hút, không hấp dẫn</p>
<p>Spending twelve hours on a plane isn't a very attractive (= pleasant) prospect.</p>
<p>an attractive offer (= an offer with benefits for me)</p>
<p>We need to make the club attractive to a wider range of people.</p>
<p>This is modern architecture at its most unattractive.</p>
<p>He was short and overweight and generally unattractive.</p>
<p>21. attractiveness (n) /əˈtræktɪvnəs/: sự hấp dẫn</p>
<p>She is well aware of her attractiveness to men.</p>
<p>Physical attractiveness is very important to some people.</p>
<p>22. attractively (adv) /əˈtræktɪvli/: hấp dẫn # unattractively (adv) /ˌʌnəˈtræktɪvli/: không hấp dẫn</p>
<p>The area offers plenty of attractively priced accommodation.</p>
<p>Most of the catwalk models were unattractively, freakishly thin.</p>
<p>When the burger arrived, it was rather unattractively soaking in its juices.</p>
<p>We always need to price our products attractively.</p>
<p>23. viewer (n) /ˈvjuːər/: người xem</p>
<p>Millions of viewers will be glued to their sets for this match.</p>
<p>24. viewable (adj) /ˈvjuːəbl/: có thể xem được</p>
<p>The film’s trailer is viewable online.</p>
<p>25. view (n) /vjuː/: quang cảnh</p>
<p>Do you have any views about /on what we should do now?</p>
<p>In my view, her criticisms were completely justified.</p>
<p>It's my view that the price is much too high.</p>
<p>Many people have /hold /share /take the view that children should not be physically punished.</p>"

<p>2. championship (n) /ˈtʃæmpiənʃɪp/: chức vô địch</p>

"<p>1. champion (n) /ˈtʃæmpiən/: nhà vô địch</p>

<p>He has been playing championship tennis for three years now.</p>
<p>3. consider (v) /kənˈsɪdər/: đánh giá, coi (là)</p>
<p>She's being considered for the job.</p>
<p>I'd like some time to consider before I make a decision.</p>

<p>As I was just saying, I think the proposal needs further consideration.</p>
<p>Three sites are presently under consideration for the new hotel.</p>
<p>I've put my proposition to the company director for his consideration.</p>
<p>The proposals that you have put forward deserve serious consideration.</p>
<p>5. considerable (adj) /kənˈsɪdərəbl/: đáng kể</p>
<p>The fire caused considerable damage to the church.</p>
<p>6. considerate (v) /kənˈsɪdərət /: thận trọng, chu đáo, ý tứ</p>
<p>It wasn't very considerate of you to drink all the milk.</p>
<p>Đối lập</p>
<p>7. considerately (adv) /kənˈsɪdərətli/: thận trọng, chu đáo, y tứ</p>
<p>She drives carefully and considerately.</p>
<p>8. considerably (adv) /kənˈsɪdərəbli/: đáng kể</p>
<p>He's considerably fatter than he was when I knew him.</p>
<p>His views differ considerably from those of his parents.</p>
<p>9. passionate (adj) /ˈpæ∫ənət /: say đắm, nồng nàn; nồng nhiệt, thiết tha</p>
<p>The child's mother made a passionate plea for help.</p>
<p>Joe is passionate about baseball (= he likes it very much).</p>
<p>10. passion (n) /ˈpæʃn/: cảm xúc mạnh mẽ, tình cảm nồng nàn</p>
<p>Football arouses a good deal of passion among its fans.</p>
<p>At school, his early interest in music developed into an abiding passion.</p>
<p>Politics and philosophy were his lifelong passions.</p>
<p>11. passionless (adj) /ˈpæʃnləs/: không sôi nổi, không say sưa, không nồng nàn, không nồng nhiệt, không thiết tha</p>
<p>They had a passionless marriage.</p>
<p>This music is passionless.</p>
<p>12. passionately (adv) /ˈpæʃənətli/: một cách say đắm, nhiệt tình; nồng nhiệt, mạnh mẽ, rất</p>
<p>Ann has always believed passionately in women's rights.</p>
<p>I feel passionately that I did the right thing.</p>
<p>13. globe (n) /ɡləʊb/: toàn cầu</p>
<p>His greatest ambition is to sail around the globe.</p>
<p>She is a superstar all around the globe.</p>
<p>14. globalize (v) /ˈɡləʊbəlaɪz/: biến thành toàn cầu, áp dụng cho cả thế giới</p>

<p>There had been hopes that the euro would lead to a golden age of economic globalism.</p>
<p>16. globalist (n) /ˈɡləʊbəlɪst /: người theo chủ nghĩa toàn cầu</p>
<p>He is a globalist, whereas we are nationalists who will put our country first.</p>
<p>She is critical of the president's globalist foreign policy.</p>

<p>We must take advantage of the increased globalization of the commodity trading business.</p>
<p>18. attract (v) /əˈtrækt /: thu hút</p>
<p>These flowers are brightly coloured in order to attract butterflies.</p>
<p>The circus is attracting huge crowds/audiences.</p>
<p>19. attraction (n) /ˌɡləʊbələˈzeɪʃn/: sự thu hút</p>
<p>Life in Los Angeles has so many attractions - nightclubs, good restaurants, and so on.</p>
<p>tourist attractions</p>

<p>Skiing holds no attraction for me.</p>
<p>20. attractive(adj) /əˈtræktɪv/: thu hút, hấp dẫn # unattractive (adj) /ˌʌnəˈtræktɪv/: không thu hút, không hấp dẫn</p>

<p>He was short and overweight and generally unattractive.</p>

<p>She is well aware of her attractiveness to men.</p>
<p>Physical attractiveness is very important to some people.</p>

"<p>1. champion (n) /ˈtʃæmpiən/: nhà vô địch</p>
<p>She is the world champion for the third year in succession.</p>
<p>The defending champion will play his first match of the tournament tomorrow.</p>
<p>Who are the reigning European football champions?</p>
<p>2. championship (n) /ˈtʃæmpiənʃɪp/: chức vô địch</p>
<p>The world championships will be held in Scotland next year.</p>
<p>He has been playing championship tennis for three years now.</p>
<p>3. consider (v) /kənˈsɪdər/: đánh giá, coi (là)</p>
<p>She's being considered for the job.</p>
<p>I'd like some time to consider before I make a decision.</p>
<p>4. consideration (n) /kənˌsɪdəˈreɪʃn/: sự xem xét</p>
<p>As I was just saying, I think the proposal needs further consideration.</p>
<p>Three sites are presently under consideration for the new hotel.</p>
<p>I've put my proposition to the company director for his consideration.</p>
<p>The proposals that you have put forward deserve serious consideration.</p>
<p>5. considerable (adj) /kənˈsɪdərəbl/: đáng kể</p>
<p>The fire caused considerable damage to the church.</p>
<p>6. considerate (v) /kənˈsɪdərət /: thận trọng, chu đáo, ý tứ</p>
<p>It wasn't very considerate of you to drink all the milk.</p>
<p>Đối lập</p>
<p>7. considerately (adv) /kənˈsɪdərətli/: thận trọng, chu đáo, y tứ</p>
<p>She drives carefully and considerately.</p>
<p>8. considerably (adv) /kənˈsɪdərəbli/: đáng kể</p>
<p>He's considerably fatter than he was when I knew him.</p>
<p>His views differ considerably from those of his parents.</p>
<p>9. passionate (adj) /ˈpæ∫ənət /: say đắm, nồng nàn; nồng nhiệt, thiết tha</p>
<p>The child's mother made a passionate plea for help.</p>
<p>Joe is passionate about baseball (= he likes it very much).</p>
<p>10. passion (n) /ˈpæʃn/: cảm xúc mạnh mẽ, tình cảm nồng nàn</p>
<p>Football arouses a good deal of passion among its fans.</p>
<p>At school, his early interest in music developed into an abiding passion.</p>
<p>Politics and philosophy were his lifelong passions.</p>
<p>11. passionless (adj) /ˈpæʃnləs/: không sôi nổi, không say sưa, không nồng nàn, không nồng nhiệt, không thiết tha</p>
<p>They had a passionless marriage.</p>
<p>This music is passionless.</p>
<p>12. passionately (adv) /ˈpæʃənətli/: một cách say đắm, nhiệt tình; nồng nhiệt, mạnh mẽ, rất</p>
<p>Ann has always believed passionately in women's rights.</p>
<p>I feel passionately that I did the right thing.</p>
<p>13. globe (n) /ɡləʊb/: toàn cầu</p>
<p>His greatest ambition is to sail around the globe.</p>
<p>She is a superstar all around the globe.</p>
<p>14. globalize (v) /ˈɡləʊbəlaɪz/: biến thành toàn cầu, áp dụng cho cả thế giới</p>
<p>Satellite broadcasting is helping to globalize television.</p>
<p>As the economy develops, it will continue to globalize.</p>
<p>15. globalism (n) /ˈɡləʊbəlɪzəm/: chủ nghĩa toàn cầu</p>
<p>There had been hopes that the euro would lead to a golden age of economic globalism.</p>
<p>16. globalist (n) /ˈɡləʊbəlɪst /: người theo chủ nghĩa toàn cầu</p>
<p>He is a globalist, whereas we are nationalists who will put our country first.</p>
<p>She is critical of the president's globalist foreign policy.</p>
<p>17. globalization (n) /ˌɡləʊbələˈzeɪʃn/: toàn cầu hóa</p>
<p>We must take advantage of the increased globalization of the commodity trading business.</p>
<p>18. attract (v) /əˈtrækt /: thu hút</p>
<p>These flowers are brightly coloured in order to attract butterflies.</p>
<p>The circus is attracting huge crowds/audiences.</p>
<p>19. attraction (n) /ˌɡləʊbələˈzeɪʃn/: sự thu hút</p>
<p>Life in Los Angeles has so many attractions - nightclubs, good restaurants, and so on.</p>
<p>tourist attractions</p>
<p>The opportunity to travel is one of the main attractions of this job.</p>
<p>Skiing holds no attraction for me.</p>
<p>20. attractive(adj) /əˈtræktɪv/: thu hút, hấp dẫn # unattractive (adj) /ˌʌnəˈtræktɪv/: không thu hút, không hấp dẫn</p>
<p>Spending twelve hours on a plane isn't a very attractive (= pleasant) prospect.</p>
<p>an attractive offer (= an offer with benefits for me)</p>
<p>We need to make the club attractive to a wider range of people.</p>
<p>This is modern architecture at its most unattractive.</p>
<p>He was short and overweight and generally unattractive.</p>
<p>21. attractiveness (n) /əˈtræktɪvnəs/: sự hấp dẫn</p>
<p>She is well aware of her attractiveness to men.</p>
<p>Physical attractiveness is very important to some people.</p>
<p>22. attractively (adv) /əˈtræktɪvli/: hấp dẫn # unattractively (adv) /ˌʌnəˈtræktɪvli/: không hấp dẫn</p>
<p>The area offers plenty of attractively priced accommodation.</p>
<p>Most of the catwalk models were unattractively, freakishly thin.</p>
<p>When the burger arrived, it was rather unattractively soaking in its juices.</p>
<p>We always need to price our products attractively.</p>
<p>23. viewer (n) /ˈvjuːər/: người xem</p>
<p>Millions of viewers will be glued to their sets for this match.</p>
<p>24. viewable (adj) /ˈvjuːəbl/: có thể xem được</p>
<p>The film’s trailer is viewable online.</p>
<p>25. view (n) /vjuː/: quang cảnh</p>
<p>Do you have any views about /on what we should do now?</p>
<p>In my view, her criticisms were completely justified.</p>
<p>It's my view that the price is much too high.</p>
<p>Many people have /hold /share /take the view that children should not be physically punished.</p>
<p>26. governing body (n) /ˈɡʌvərnɪŋ ˈbɑːdi/: cơ quan quản lí</p>
<p>The country's highest governing body held a special meeting to consider the proposal.</p>
<p>governing body of sth Officials criticized the FIA, the governing body of motor sport, over the sensitive issue of safety</p>
<p>27. governance (n) /ˈɡʌvərnəns/: sự cai trị; sự cai quản</p>
<p>He emphasized the company's commitment to high standards of corporate governance.</p>
<p>The aim is to include representatives of all ethnic groups in the governance of the new state.</p>
<p>The government is stressing the link between aid and good governance in poor countries.</p>
<p>28. governess (n) /ˈɡʌvərnəs/: người đàn bà được thuê dạy cho trẻ em tại nhà của chúng và sống như một thành viên trong gia đình của chúng; nữ gia sư</p>
<p>She was educated at home by a series of governesses.</p>
<p>She was governess to the three daughters of a wealthy manufacturer.</p>
<p>29. government (n) /ˈɡʌvərnmənt /: chính phủ</p>
<p>The government is/are expected to announce its/their tax proposals today.</p>
<p>The minister has announced that there will be no change in government policy.</p>
<p>Senior government officials will be attending a meeting tomorrow.</p>
<p>Theatre companies are very concerned about cuts in government grants to the arts.</p>
<p>30. governmental (adj) /ˌɡʌvərnˈmentl/:thuộc hoặc có quan hệ với chính quyền</p>
<p>We await a governmental decision about the future of the programme.</p>
<p>31. governor (n) /ˈɡʌvərnər/: thống đốc</p>
<p>The governor exhorted the prisoners not to riot.</p>
<p>The governor was looking for a fall guy to take the blame for the corruption scandal.</p>
<p>The governor has denied making improper use of state money.</p>
<p>32. govern (v) /ˈɡʌvərn/: quản lý, cai trị</p>
<p>We are governed, in Lord Hailsham's famous phrase, by an 'elective dictatorship'.</p>
<p>The country's being governed by a bunch of incompetents.</p>
<p>He was chosen to govern the colony by the British government.</p>
<p>He has been governing the country since taking power in a military coup.</p>
<p>33. compete (v) /kəmˈpiːt /: cạnh tranh</p>
<p>It's difficult for a small shop to compete against /with the big supermarkets.</p>
<p>Both girls compete for their father's attention.</p>
<p>34. competence (n) /ˈkɑːmpɪtəns/: năng lực</p>
<p>Her competence as a teacher is unquestionable.</p>
<p>He reached a reasonable level of competence in his English.</p>
<p>35. competency (n) /ˈkɑːmpɪtənsi/: có khả năng</p>
<p>Once the informal competency questions are available, the set of terms used can be extracted from the questions.</p>
<p>36. competent (adj) /ˈkɑːmpɪtənt /: có thẩm quyền</p>
<p>I wouldn't say he was brilliant but he is competent at his job.</p>
<p>37. competently (adv) /ˈkɑːmpɪtənt /: thành thạo</p>
<p>I thought she played the role very competently.</p>
<p>He failed to represent his clients competently.</p>
<p>38. elimination games /ɪˌlɪmɪˈneɪʃn ɡeɪmz/: các trận đấu loại</p>
<p>In sports, an elimination game is a game that decides which team or player will take part in the next stage of a particular competition.</p>
<p>39. eliminate (v) /ɪˈlɪmɪneɪt /: loại bỏ, bài tiết</p>
<p>A move towards healthy eating could help eliminate heart disease.</p>
<p>We eliminated the possibility that it could have been an accident.</p>
<p>The police eliminated him from their enquiries.</p>
<p>40. finalist (n) /ˈfaɪnəlɪst /: đội vào vòng chung kết</p>
<p>This year's finalists and award winners appear to be no exception.</p>
<p>Ultimately, four finalists were chosen with a limited edition of each cover going into circulation.</p>
<p>41. final (adj) /ˈfaɪnl/: cuối cùng</p>
<p>The project is in its final stages and should be completed by August.</p>
<p>The final figures showed that most departments had stayed within budget.</p>
<p>That's my final offer - you can take it or leave it.</p>
<p>42. finalize (v) /ˈfaɪnəlaɪz/: cho hình dạng cuối cùng, làm cho hình thành hình dạng cuối cùng; thông qua lần cuối cùng,  vào vòng chung kết</p>
<p>Details of the deal are being finalized.</p>
<p>43. finality (n) /faɪˈnæləti/: tính dứt khoác, chung cuộc</p>
<p>The finality of death is sometimes hard to accept.</p>
<p>44. finalization (n) /faɪˈnæləti/: sự hoàn thiện</p>
<p>Finalization of the agreement was first reported online.</p>
<p>45. honored (adj) /ˈɑːnərd /: vinh dự</p>
<p>t's an honor to have you here today, Mr President.</p>
<p>Great honor attaches to winning this award.</p>
<p>The party was held in honor of Vivienne Westwood, that doyenne of British fashion.</p>
<p>46. honorable (adj) /ˈɑːnərəbl/: xứng đáng, mang đến hoặc thể hiện danh dự, danh giá</p>
<p>But they required that the transfer of power be unhurried, orderly, and honorable.</p>
<p>47. honorably(adv) /ˈɑːnərəbli/: danh dự</p>
<p>I wanted us to behave honorably, truthfully.</p>
<p>Millions served honorablyin the war.</p>
<p>48. honoree (n) /ˌɑːnəˈriː/: người được vinh danh</p>
<p>Stevie Wonder was among the honorees at the annual Songwriters Hall of Fame Awards ceremony.</p>
<p>49. honor (n) /ˈɑːnər/: tôn kính, danh dự</p>

<p>Great honor attaches to winning this award.</p>
<p>The party was held in honor of Vivienne Westwood, that doyenne of British fashion.</p>
<p>It's an honor to meet you Sir.</p>
<p>50. involve (v) /ɪnˈvɑːlv/: liên quan</p>
<p>The plot of the film was too involved - I couldn't understand it.</p>
<p>I prefer teaching methods that actively involve students in learning.</p>
<p>She's been involved with animal rights for many years.</p>
<p>It would be difficult not to involve the child's father in the arrangements.</p>
<p>51. involved (adj) /ɪnˈvɑːlvd /: bị liên lụy</p>
<p>The plot of the film was too involved - I couldn't understand it.</p>
<p>52. involvement (n) /ɪnˈvɑːlvmənt /: sự tham gia</p>
<p>The team's continued involvement in the competition is uncertain.</p>
<p>Being on the committee is one involvement I could do without.</p>
<p>53. facility (n) /fəˈsɪləti/: thiết bị</p>
<p>rotesters have been demonstrating outside the new research facility.</p>
<p>The training facility is scheduled to open in April 2005.</p>
<p>New vehicles are inspected at the company's inspection facility.</p>
<p>54. facilitate (v) /fəˈsɪlɪteɪt /: làm cho dễ dàng; làm cho thuận tiện</p>
<p>The new ramp will facilitate the entry of wheelchairs.</p>
<p>The current structure does not facilitate efficient work flow.</p>
<p>55. facilitation (n) /fəˌsɪlɪˈteɪʃn/: tạo điều kiện</p>
<p>Airports are interested in the facilitation of the movement of people.</p>
<p>This team building can involve some form of outside help or facilitation.</p>
<p>The panel also urges better monitoring and facilitation of the voting process.</p>
<p>56. facilitator (n) /fəˈsɪlɪteɪtər/: người điều hành</p>
<p>I see my role as that of a facilitator, enabling other people to work in the way that suits them best.</p>
<p>57. promote (v) /prəˈməʊt /: thúc đẩy</p>

<p>58. promoter (n) /prəˈməʊtər/: người ủng hộ</p>
<p>The country is now a leading promoter of regional trade.</p>
<p>He was a promoter of education and the arts.</p>
<p>59. promotion (n) /prəˈməʊʃn/: khuyến mãi</p>
<p>There was a promotion in the supermarket and they were giving away free glasses of wine.</p>
<p>Obviously as sales manager he'll be very involved in the promotion and marketing of the product.</p>
<p>60. promotional (adj) /prəˈməʊʃənl/: (thuộc) quảng cáo (để bán hàng..)</p>
<p>The writer recently went on a promotional tour of his homeland.</p>
<p>61. retirement (n) /rɪˈtaɪərmənt /: sự về hưu</p>
<p>Many teachers over the age of 50 are taking early retirement.</p>
<p>What is the normal retirement age in this country?</p>
<p>62. retiree (n) /rɪˌtaɪəˈriː/: người về hưu</p>
<p>Most retirees underestimate their actual financial needs.</p>
<p>The airline's pension fund has been paying out more than $500 million a year to retirees.</p>
<p>Workers' annual cost-of-living raises will be diverted to help pay for retiree health care.</p>
<p>63. retire (v) /rɪˈtaɪər/: về hưu</p>
<p>He is retiring next year after 30 years with the company.</p>
<p>The company's official retiring age is 65.</p>
<p>Lots of teachers like me expected to retire on a full pension.</p>
<p>64. retired (adj) /rɪˈtaɪərd /: nghỉ hưu, ẩn dật</p>
<p>Both my parents are retired.</p>
<p>He is a retired airline pilot.</p>
<p>65. committee (n) /kəˈmɪti/: ủy ban</p>
<p>She sits on/is on the school's development committee.</p>
<p>The local council has just set up a committee to study recycling.</p>
<p>66. commit (v) /kəˈmɪt /: hứa, cam đoan</p>
<p>Soldiers who obey orders to commit atrocities should be answerable for their crimes.</p>
<p>They were imprisoned for incitement to commit grievous bodily harm.</p>
<p>Fresh evidence has recently come to light which suggests that he didn't in fact commit the murder.</p>
<p>67. commitment (n) /kəˈmɪtmənt /: sự cam kết</p>
<p>Players must make a commitment to play for a full season.</p>
<p>Can you give a commitment that the money will be made available?</p>
<p>The government reaffirmed its commitment to the peace process.</p>
<p>The company has failed to honor its commitments.</p>
<p>68. committal (n) /kəˈmɪtl/: ủy nhiệm, giao phó # noncommittal (adj) /ˌnɑːn kəˈmɪtl/: không cam kết, không giao phó</p>
<p>The psychiatric team decided that committal would not be beneficial in her case.</p>
<p>69. announce (v) /əˈnaʊns/: thông báo</p>
<p>They announced the death of their mother in the local paper.</p>
<p>She announced the winner of the competition to an excited audience.</p>
<p>70. announcement (n) /əˈnaʊnsmənt /: sự thông báo, lời rao</p>
<p>Her announcement confirmed (that) she would be resigning as prime minister.</p>
<p>The protests are a delayed reaction to last week's announcement.</p>
<p>The announcement took Washington and Paris by surprise, but Downing Street had been expecting it.</p>
<p>71. announcer (n) /əˈnaʊnsər/: phát thanh viên</p>
<p>In other words, the fact that the announcer performs a particular role does not explain the nature of that role.</p>
<p>72. postpone (v) /pəʊˈspəʊn/: hoãn lại</p>
<p>They decided to postpone their holiday until next year.</p>
<p>We've had to postpone going to France because the children are ill.</p>
<p>73. postponement (n) /pəʊˈspəʊnmənt /: sự trì hoãn</p>
<p>His lawyers requested a postponement of his trial.</p>
<p>Professional sports announced mass postponements and cancellations.</p>
<p>An indefinite postponement was ordered by the judge because of the danger posed by a violent protest taking place outside the courthouse.</p>
<p>74. severe (adj) /sɪˈvɪr/: khắc nghiệt</p>
<p>This is a school for children with severe learning difficulties.</p>
<p>In parts of Africa there is a severe food /water shortage.</p>
<p>There is expected to be a severe frost tonight.</p>
<p>75. severely (adv) /sɪˈvɪrli/: khắt khe, gay gắt (trong thái độ, cách cư xử); ất xấu, rất mãnh liệt, rất gay go, khốc liệt, dữ dội</p>
<p>Their movements have been severely circumscribed since the laws came into effect.</p>
<p>The arms-dealing affair has severely damaged the reputation of the government.</p>
<p>The last government severely curtailed trade union rights.</p>
<p>The accident left him severely disabled.</p>
<p>76. severity (n) /sɪˈverəti/: tính nghiêm khắc; tính nghiêm nghị; sự ngặt nghèo, tính mộc mạc, tính giản dị</p>
<p>Even the doctors were shocked by the severity of his injuries.</p>
<p>I don't think you quite understand the severity of our financial problems.</p>
<p>77. contact (v) /ˈkɑːntækt /: liên hệ</p>
<p>&quot;Have you been in contact with Andrew recently?&quot; &quot;Only by phone.&quot;</p>
<p>I'm still in contact with her - we write a couple of times a year.</p>
<p>There isn't enough contact between teachers and parents.</p>
<p>78. contactable (adj) /ˈkɑːntæktəbl/; có thể tiếp cận được</p>
<p>Is he contactable at his home number?</p>
<p>80 percent of Australian people are contactable by mobile phone.</p>
<p>79. contactee (n) /ˌkɑːntækˈtiː/: người tiếp xúc</p>
<p>Contactees are persons who claim to have experienced contact with extraterrestrials.</p>"

<p>11. originally /əˈrɪdʒənəli/ (adv): bắt đầu, khởi đầu, từ lúc bắt đầu, một cách sáng tạo, mới mẻ, độc đáo</p>

<p>25. formality (n) /fɔːrˈmæləti/: sự theo đúng quy cách, sự theo đúng thủ tục, nghi lễ, nghi thức, thủ tục, lề thói; sự trang trọng</p>
<p>26. formalist (n) /ˈfɔːrməlɪst /: người quá câu nệ hình thức</p>
<p>27. formalization (n) /ˌfɔːrmələˈzeɪʃn/: sự nghi thức hoá, sự trang trọng hoá, sự chính thức hoá</p>"
"<p>1. metropolitan /ˌmetrəˈpɑːlɪtən/ (adj): thuộc về khu đô thị</p>
<p>He was drawn to the metropolitan glamour and excitement of Paris.</p>
<p>2. metropolis (n) /məˈtrɑːpəlɪs/: thủ phủ chính của một vùng hoặc một nước; thủ đô</p>
<p>Soon afterwards he left to begin his career in the metropolis.</p>
<p>3. region /ˈri:dʒən/ (n): khu vực</p>
<p>There's a shortage of cheap housing in the region.</p>
<p>4. regional (adj) /ˈriːdʒənl/: (thuộc) vùng; địa phương</p>
<p>The regional editions of the paper contain specific information for that area.</p>
<p>The three nations competed for regional hegemony.</p>
<p>The poll showed that 80% of the population supported regional self-government.</p>
<p>5. regionally (adv) /ˈriːdʒənəli/: (thuộc) vùng; địa phương khu vực</p>
<p>The organization runs several regionally based projects.</p>
<p>The nation remains deeply divided, politically and regionally.</p>
<p>6. regionalism (n) /ˈriːdʒənəlɪzəm/: chủ nghĩa khu vực</p>
<p>&quot;Spider&quot; is a New England regionalism for a type of frying pan.</p>
<p>7. finance /ˈfaɪnæns/ (n): tài chính</p>
<p>You need to speak to someone in the finance department.</p>
<p>The finance committee controls the school's budget.</p>
<p>8. financial (adj) faɪˈnænʃl/: thuộc về tài chính</p>
<p>She organizes her financial affairs very efficiently.</p>
<p>He steered the country through a financial crisis.</p>
<p>Is there any hope of getting financial support for the project?</p>
<p>The company needs more financial assistance from the government.</p>
<p>9. financially (adv) /faɪˈnænʃəli/: về tài chính</p>
<p>Financially, this year has been one of the best years for the festival.</p>
<p>The district continues to struggle financially.</p>
<p>They have been financially destroyed by losing their entire pension.</p>
<p>10. financier (n) /ˌfɪnənˈsɪr/: chuyên gia tài chính, nhà tư bản tài chính, nhà tài phiệt</p>
<p>The millionaire financier agreed to invest $500 million in the ailing company.</p>
<p>11. originally /əˈrɪdʒənəli/ (adv): bắt đầu, khởi đầu, từ lúc bắt đầu, một cách sáng tạo, mới mẻ, độc đáo</p>
<p>The building was originally Victorian in design.</p>
<p>The city grew up originally as a crossing point on the river.</p>
<p>The novel was originally published in hardcover.</p>
<p>It was Bob who originally put up the idea of the exhibition.</p>
<p>New York was originally a Dutch trading post.</p>
<p>12. origin (n) /ˈɔːrɪdʒɪn/: nguồn gốc, căn nguyên, khởi nguyên, dòng dõi, lai lịch</p>
<p>It's a book about the origin of the universe.</p>
<p>Her unhappy childhood was the origin of her problems later in life.</p>
<p>What's the origin of this saying? (= Where did it come from?)</p>
<p>13. original (adj) /əˈrɪdʒənl/: nguyên bản</p>
<p>We agreed to look afresh at her original proposal.</p>
<p>This is a daring new film by one of our most original modern directors.</p>
<p>My original statement has been completely distorted by the media.</p>
<p>Researchers tried many times to replicate the original experiment.</p>
<p>14. originality (n) /əˌrɪdʒəˈnæləti/: sự độc đáo</p>
<p>We were impressed by the originality of the children's work.</p>
<p>15. originate (v) /əˈrɪdʒɪneɪt /: bắt nguồn từ, phát minh; sáng chế; tạo ra</p>
<p>Although the technology originated in the UK, it has been developed in the US</p>
<p>The game is thought to have originated among the native peoples of Alaska.</p>
<p>16. origination (n) /əˌrɪdʒɪˈneɪʃn/: nguồn gốc, nguyên nhân</p>
<p>Profits from the mortgage origination business will probably slow in the near term.</p>
<p>17. originator (n) /əˈrɪdʒɪneɪtər/: người khởi xướng</p>
<p>There are lots of reasons why the inventor or originator of an idea may not get the lion's share of the rewards.</p>
<p>18. transport (n) /ˈtrænspɔːrt /: giao thông</p>
<p>Do you have your own transport (= vehicle)?</p>
<p>Bicycles are a cheap and efficient form/means of transport.</p>
<p>19. transportation (n) /ˌtrænspərˈteɪʃn/: vận tải</p>
<p>t's an ecologically friendly means of transportation.</p>
<p>We need to find some other means of transportation.</p>
<p>The transportation of live animals is a controversial issue.</p>
<p>20. transporter (n) /trænˈspɔːrtər/: người chuyên chở</p>
<p>Transporters that handle asbestos products often face personal injury allegations.</p>
<p>21. transportable (adj) /trænˈspɔːrtəbl/: có thể vận chuyển</p>
<p>They are ubiquitous in seasonal and perennial wetlands and are easily transportable after drying into cakes.</p>
<p>22. transport (v) /trænˈspɔːrt /: vận chuyển</p>
<p>his delightful musical comedy transports the audience to the innocent days of 1950s America.</p>
<p>23. formal /ˈfɔːrml/ (adj): hình thức, trang trọng</p>
<p>They wanted to make a formal complaint about their doctor.</p>
<p>The US lodged a formal protest against the arrest of the foreign reporters.</p>
<p>24. formalize (v) /ˈfɔːrməlaɪz/: chính thức hóa</p>
<p>These informal gatherings have become increasingly formalized in the last few years.</p>
<p>They offered me the job, but the contract has not been formalized yet.</p>
<p>25. formality (n) /fɔːrˈmæləti/: sự theo đúng quy cách, sự theo đúng thủ tục, nghi lễ, nghi thức, thủ tục, lề thói; sự trang trọng</p>
<p>We'll have to observe the formalities (= do what is expected).</p>
<p>26. formalist (n) /ˈfɔːrməlɪst /: người quá câu nệ hình thức</p>
<p>Not that the writer is by any means a rigid formalist.</p>
<p>27. formalization (n) /ˌfɔːrmələˈzeɪʃn/: sự nghi thức hoá, sự trang trọng hoá, sự chính thức hoá</p>
<p>The aim is to provide insight into the more rigorous formalization that will be provided in the following sections.</p>"
"<p>1. metropolitan /ˌmetrəˈpɑːlɪtən/ (adj): thuộc về khu đô thị</p>
<p>2. metropolis (n) /məˈtrɑːpəlɪs/: thủ phủ chính của một vùng hoặc một nước; thủ đô</p>
<p>3. region /ˈri:dʒən/ (n): khu vực</p>

<p>15. originate (v) /əˈrɪdʒɪneɪt /: bắt nguồn từ, phát minh; sáng chế; tạo ra</p>
<p>16. origination (n) /əˌrɪdʒɪˈneɪʃn/: nguồn gốc, nguyên nhân</p>
<p>17. originator (n) /əˈrɪdʒɪneɪtər/: người khởi xướng</p>

<p>20. transporter (n) /trænˈspɔːrtər/: người chuyên chở</p>

<p>28. reserved /rɪˈzɜːrvd / (adj): dè dặt, kín đáo, đã dành trước; dành riêng # unreserved (adj) /ˌʌnrɪˈzɜːrvd /: không dành riêng, không cấp trước cho một người nhất định không hạn chế, hoàn toàn, không còn giữ lại cái gì</p>
<p>29. reserve (n/v) /rɪˈzɜːrv/: dự trữ</p>
<p>30. reservation (n) /ˌrezərˈveɪʃn/: dự phòng</p>
<p>31. reservist (n) /rɪˈzɜːrvɪst /: người dự bị, dự trữ, lính dự bị (của một quốc gia)</p>
<p>32. convenient /kənˈviːniənt / (for sb/ sth) (adj): thuận tiện</p>

<p>35. familiar /fəˈmɪliər/ (adj): quen thuộc</p>
<p>36. familiarity (n) /fəˌmɪliˈærəti/: sự quen thuộc</p>
<p>37. familiarization (n) /fəˌmɪliərəˈzeɪʃn/: sự phổ biến (một vấn đề), sự làm cho quen (với vấn đề gì, công việc gì...)</p>
<p>38. familiarize (v) /fəˈmɪliəraɪz/: làm quen, làm cho hiểu biết đầy đủ về cái gì</p>
<p>39. familiarly (adv) /fəˈmɪliərli/: thân mật; thân tình</p>
<p>40. enlighten /ɪnˈlaɪtn/ (v): khai sáng</p>
<p>41. enlightened (adj) /ɪnˈlaɪtnd /: được giải thoát khỏi thành kiến, khỏi sự ngu dốt và mê tín; được khai sáng; ngộ đạo</p>
<p>42. enlightening (adj) /ɪnˈlaɪtnɪŋ/: khai sáng, giáo huấn</p>
<p>43. enlightenment (n) /ɪnˈlaɪtnmənt /: sự khai sáng hoặc được khai sáng</p>
<p>44. ideal /aɪˈdiːəl/ (adj): lí tưởng</p>
<p>45. idealize (v) /aɪˈdiːəlaɪz/: lý tưởng hóa</p>
<p>46. ideally (adv) /aɪˈdiːəli/: lý tưởng</p>
<p>47. idealization (n) /aɪˌdiːələˈzeɪʃn/: sự lý tưởng hóa</p>
<p>48. idealism (n) /aɪˈdiːəlɪzəm/: chủ nghĩa duy tâm</p>
<p>49. idealistic (adj) /ˌaɪdiəˈlɪstɪk/: duy tâm</p>
<p>50. idealist (n) /aɪˈdiːəlɪst /: người hay lý tưởng hoá; (mỉa mai) người mơ mộng không thực tế</p>"

<p>28. reserved /rɪˈzɜːrvd / (adj): dè dặt, kín đáo, đã dành trước; dành riêng # unreserved (adj) /ˌʌnrɪˈzɜːrvd /: không dành riêng, không cấp trước cho một người nhất định không hạn chế, hoàn toàn, không còn giữ lại cái gì</p>
<p>Critics expressed unreserved enthusiasm for the book.</p>
<p>The English have a reputation for being reserved.</p>
<p>29. reserve (n/v) /rɪˈzɜːrv/: dự trữ</p>
<p>I reserve Mondays for tidying my desk and answering letters.</p>
<p>These seats are reserved for the elderly and women with babies.</p>
<p>30. reservation (n) /ˌrezərˈveɪʃn/: dự phòng</p>
<p>I'd like to make a table reservation for two people for nine o'clock.</p>
<p>Please confirm your reservation in writing by Friday.</p>
<p>31. reservist (n) /rɪˈzɜːrvɪst /: người dự bị, dự trữ, lính dự bị (của một quốc gia)</p>
<p>The reservist is normally notified whether he is fit or unfit for recall within 15 days of his medical examination.</p>
<p>32. convenient /kənˈviːniənt / (for sb/ sth) (adj): thuận tiện</p>
<p>Our local shop has very convenient opening hours.</p>
<p>A bike's a very convenient way of getting around.</p>
<p>33. convenience (n) /kənˈviːniəns/: tiện nghi</p>
<p>I like the convenience of living close to work.</p>
<p>Just for convenience, I'm going to live at my mother's place until my new apartment is ready.</p>
<p>34. conveniently (adv) /kənˈviːniəntli/: thuận tiện</p>
<p>They have conveniently provided a return envelope for you to use.</p>
<p>The box conveniently folds flat when not in use.</p>
<p>35. familiar /fəˈmɪliər/ (adj): quen thuộc</p>
<p>There were one or two familiar faces (= people I knew).</p>

"<p>1.        Ho Chi Minhˈs Mausoleum /mɔ:səˈliəm/: Lăng Chủ tịch Hồ Chí Minh</p>
<p>The President Ho Chi Minh Mausoleum is a mausoleum which serves as the resting place of Vietnamese Revolutionary leader and President Ho Chi Minh in Hanoi, Vietnam.It is a large building located in the center of Ba Dinh Square, where Ho, Chairman of the Workers' Party of Vietnam from 1951 until his death in 1969, read the Declaration of Independence on 2 September 1945, establishing the Democratic Republic of Vietnam. It is open to the public.</p>

<p>Independence Palace, also publicly known as Reunification Convention Hall, is a landmark in Ho Chi Minh City (formerly known as Saigon), Vietnam. It was designed by architect Ngô Viết Thụ and was the home and workplace of the President of Republic of (South) Vietnam. It was the site of the Fall of Saigon on 30 April 1975 that ended the Vietnam War, when a North Vietnamese Army tank crashed through its gates.</p>

<p>The artist formerly known as Prince.</p>

<p>The house was formerly owned by the local council.</p>
<p>12.        trading /ˈtreidiη/ (n): thương mại, buôn bán</p>
<p>The stock market moved ahead slightly in active trading today.</p>
<p>13.        tile roofed (adj): mái nhà được lợp ngói</p>
<p>It is a three-storey house with an old tiled roof but with no felt lining underneath that roof.</p>
<p>14.        recommend /rekəˈmend / (v): gợi ý, đề nghị</p>
<p>I can recommend the chicken in mushroom sauce - it's delicious.</p>
<p>She has been recommended for promotion.</p>
<p>The headmistress agreed to recommend the teachers' proposals to the school governors.</p>
<p>15.        Assembly Hall of Cantonese /əˈsembli hɔːl əv ˌkæntəˈniːz/ = Chinese Congregation /ˌtʃaɪˈniːz ˌkɑːŋɡrɪˈɡeɪʃn/: Hội Quán Quảng Châu.</p>
<p>Cantonese Assembly Hall (Hoi Quan Quang Dong in Vietnamese) is located on Tran Phu Street which is home to many unique architectural works of great historical value. Conveniently located near Japanese Covered Bridge (Chua Cau), this style-mingled assembly hall welcomes flocks of visitors on a daily basis, adding a dash of color to the multicolored Hoi An.</p>
<p>16.        precious (adj) /ˈˈpreʃəs/: quý giá</p>
<p>Clean water is a precious commodity in many parts of the world.</p>
<p>17.        Tan Ky House: Ngôi nhà Tấn Ký</p>
<p> Tan Ky Old House was built in 1741. It is the place where 7 generations of Le family have lived.</p>
<p>18.        Japanese Covered Bridge /ˌdʒæpəˈniːz ˈkʌvərd brɪdʒ/: Chùa cầu Nhật Bản</p>
<p> The Japanese Covered Bridge was built over the Thu Bon river in Hoi An, while the temple was located on the Northside of the bridge.</p>
<p>19.        chart /tʃɑːrt / (n): biểu đồ </p>
<p>There is a chart on the classroom wall showing the relative heights of all the children.</p>
<p>The sales chart shows a distinct decline in the past few months.</p>"
